Itle:tay Omeoray anday Ulietjay

EtHay AGEDYtRay OFay OMEOray ANDay ULIETjay

ybay Illiamway Akespeareshay




Ontentscay

EtHay OLOGUEpRay.

ACTay Iay
Enescay I.ay Aay ublicpay aceplay.
Enescay II.ay Aay Eetstray.
Enescay III.ay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay IV.ay Aay Eetstray.
Enescay vay. Aay Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

ACTay IIay
ORUScHay.
Enescay I.ay Anay openay aceplay adjoiningay Apulet’scay Ardengay.
Enescay II.ay Apulet’scay Ardengay.
Enescay III.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.
Enescay IV.ay Aay Eetstray.
Enescay vay. Apulet’scay Ardengay.
Enescay Ivay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.

ACTay IIIay
Enescay I.ay Aay ublicpay Aceplay.
Enescay II.ay Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay III.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay ellcay.
Enescay IV.ay Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay vay. Anay openay Allerygay otay Uliet’sjay Amber,chay overlookingay ethay Ardengay.

ACTay IVay
Enescay I.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.
Enescay II.ay Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay III.ay Uliet’sjay Amberchay.
Enescay IV.ay Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.
Enescay vay. Uliet’sjay Amber;chay Ulietjay onay ethay edbay.

ACTay vay
Enescay I.ay Antuamay. Aay Eetstray.
Enescay II.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.
Enescay III.ay Aay urchyard;chay inay itay aay Onumentmay elongingbay otay ethay Apuletscay.




Amatisdray Ersonæpay

ESCALUS,ay Incepray ofay Eronavay.
ERCUTIO,may insmankay otay ethay Ince,pray anday iendfray otay Omeoray.
ARIS,pay aay youngay Obleman,nay insmankay otay ethay Incepray.
Agepay otay Arispay.

ONTAGUE,may eadhay ofay aay Eronesevay amilyfay atay eudfay ithway ethay Apuletscay.
ADYlay ONTAGUE,may ifeway otay Ontaguemay.
OMEO,ray onsay otay Ontaguemay.
ENVOLIO,bay ephewnay otay Ontague,may anday iendfray otay Omeoray.
ABRAM,ay ervantsay otay Ontaguemay.
ALTHASAR,bay ervantsay otay Omeoray.

APULET,cay eadhay ofay aay Eronesevay amilyfay atay eudfay ithway ethay Ontaguesmay.
ADYlay APULET,cay ifeway otay Apuletcay.
ULIET,jay aughterday otay Apuletcay.
YBALT,tay ephewnay otay Adylay Apuletcay.
APULET’Scay OUSIN,cay anay olday anmay.
URSEnay otay Ulietjay.
ETER,pay ervantsay otay Uliet’sjay Ursenay.
AMPSON,say ervantsay otay Apuletcay.
EGORY,gRay ervantsay otay Apuletcay.
Ervantssay.

IARfRay AWRENCE,lay aay Anciscanfray.
IARfRay OHN,jay ofay ethay amesay Order.ay
Anay Apothecary.ay
ORUScHay.
Eethray Usiciansmay.
Anay Officer.ay
Itizenscay ofay Erona;vay everalsay Enmay anday Omen,way elationsray otay othbay ouses;hay
Askers,may Uards,gay Atchmenway anday Attendants.ay

ENEsCay. Uringday ethay eatergray artpay ofay ethay Ayplay inay Erona;vay once,ay inay ethay
Ifthfay Act,ay atay Antuamay.




EtHay OLOGUEpRay


Enteray Oruschay.

ORUScHay.
Otway ouseholds,hay othbay alikeay inay ignity,day
Inay airfay Erona,vay erewhay eway aylay ouray ene,scay
Omfray ancientay udgegray eakbray otay ewnay utiny,may
Erewhay ivilcay oodblay akesmay ivilcay andshay unclean.ay
Omfray orthfay ethay atalfay oinslay ofay esethay otway oesfay
Aay airpay ofay ar-cross’dstay overslay aketay eirthay ife;lay
Osewhay isadventur’dmay iteouspay overthrowsay
Othday ithway eirthay eathday urybay eirthay arents’pay ifestray.
Ethay earfulfay assagepay ofay eirthay eath-mark’dday ove,lay
Anday ethay ontinuancecay ofay eirthay arents’pay age,ray
Ich,whay utbay eirthay ildren’schay end,ay oughtnay ouldcay emove,ray
Isay ownay ethay otway ours’hay affictray ofay ouray age;stay
Ethay ich,whay ifay youay ithway atientpay earsay attend,ay
Atwhay erehay allshay iss,may ouray oiltay allshay ivestray otay endmay.

Exit._][_ay




ACTay Iay

ENEsCay I.ay Aay ublicpay aceplay.


Enteray Ampsonsay anday Egorygray armeday ithway ordssway anday ucklersbay.

AMPSONsay.
Egory,gray onay ymay ord,way e’llway otnay arrycay oalscay.

EGORYgRay.
O,nay orfay enthay eway ouldshay ebay ollierscay.

AMPSONsay.
Iay ean,may ifay eway ebay inay oler,chay e’llway awdray.

EGORYgRay.
Ay,ay ilewhay youay ive,lay awdray youray ecknay outay o’ay ethay ollarcay.

AMPSONsay.
Iay ikestray uickly,qay eingbay ovedmay.

EGORYgRay.
Utbay outhay artay otnay uicklyqay ovedmay otay ikestray.

AMPSONsay.
Aay ogday ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguemay ovesmay emay.

EGORYgRay.
Otay ovemay isay otay ir;stay anday otay ebay aliantvay isay otay and:stay erefore,thay ifay outhay
artay oved,may outhay unn’stray away.ay

AMPSONsay.
Aay ogday ofay atthay ousehay allshay ovemay emay otay andstay.
Iay illway aketay ethay allway ofay anyay anmay oray aidmay ofay Ontague’smay.

EGORYgRay.
Atthay owsshay eethay aay eakway ave,slay orfay ethay eakestway oesgay otay ethay allway.

AMPSONsay.
Ue,tray anday ereforethay omen,way eingbay ethay eakerway essels,vay areay everay ustthray otay
ethay all:way ereforethay Iay illway ushpay Ontague’smay enmay omfray ethay all,way anday
ustthray ishay aidsmay otay ethay allway.

EGORYgRay.
Ethay uarrelqay isay etweenbay ouray astersmay anday usay eirthay enmay.

AMPSONsay.
Is’Tay allay one,ay Iay illway owshay yselfmay aay yrant:tay enwhay Iay avehay oughtfay ithway ethay
enmay Iay illway ebay ivilcay ithway ethay aids,may Iay illway utcay offay eirthay eadshay.

EGORYgRay.
Ethay eadshay ofay ethay aids?may

AMPSONsay.
Ay,ay ethay eadshay ofay ethay aids,may oray eirthay aidenheads;may aketay itay inay atwhay ensesay
outhay iltway.

EGORYgRay.
Eythay ustmay aketay itay inay ensesay atthay eelfay it.ay

AMPSONsay.
Emay eythay allshay eelfay ilewhay Iay amay ableay otay and:stay anday Is’tay ownknay Iay amay aay
ettypray iecepay ofay eshflay.

EGORYgRay.
Is’Tay ellway outhay artay otnay ish;fay ifay outhay adst,hay outhay adsthay eenbay oorpay Ohnjay.
Awdray ythay ool;tay erehay omescay ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontaguesmay.

Enteray Abramay anday Althasarbay.

AMPSONsay.
Ymay akednay eaponway isay out:ay uarrel,qay Iay illway ackbay eethay.

EGORYgRay.
Ow?hay Urntay ythay ackbay anday un?ray

AMPSONsay.
Earfay emay otnay.

EGORYgRay.
O,nay arry;may Iay earfay ee!thay

AMPSONsay.
Etlay usay aketay ethay awlay ofay ouray ides;say etlay emthay eginbay.

EGORYgRay.
Iay illway ownfray asay Iay asspay y,bay anday etlay emthay aketay itay asay eythay istlay.

AMPSONsay.
Ay,nay asay eythay areday. Iay illway itebay ymay umbthay atay em,thay ichwhay isay isgraceday otay
emthay ifay eythay earbay it.ay

ABRAM.ay
Oday youay itebay youray umbthay atay us,ay ir?say

AMPSONsay.
Iay oday itebay ymay umb,thay irsay.

ABRAM.ay
Oday youay itebay youray umbthay atay us,ay ir?say

AMPSONsay.
Isay ethay awlay ofay ouray idesay ifay Iay aysay ay?ay

EGORYgRay.
Onay.

AMPSONsay.
Onay ir,say Iay oday otnay itebay ymay umbthay atay you,ay ir;say utbay Iay itebay ymay umb,thay irsay.

EGORYgRay.
Oday youay uarrel,qay ir?say

ABRAM.ay
Uarrel,qay ir?say O,nay irsay.

AMPSONsay.
Utbay ifay youay o,day ir,say Iay amay orfay you.ay Iay ervesay asay oodgay aay anmay asay you.ay

ABRAM.ay
Onay etterbay.

AMPSONsay.
Ell,way irsay.

Enteray Envoliobay.

EGORYgRay.
Aysay etter;bay erehay omescay oneay ofay ymay aster’smay insmenkay.

AMPSONsay.
Yes,ay etter,bay irsay.

ABRAM.ay
Youay ielay.

AMPSONsay.
Aw,dray ifay youay ebay enmay. Egory,gray ememberray ythay ashingway owblay.

Ey[_Thay ight._]fay

ENVOLIObay.
Art,pay ools!fay utpay upay youray ords,sway youay owknay otnay atwhay youay oday.

Eats[_Bay ownday eirthay ords._]sway

Enteray Ybalttay.

YBALTtay.
At,whay artay outhay awndray amongay esethay eartlesshay inds?hay
Urntay eethay Envolio,bay ooklay uponay ythay eathday.

ENVOLIObay.
Iay oday utbay eepkay ethay eace,pay utpay upay ythay ord,sway
Oray anagemay itay otay artpay esethay enmay ithway emay.

YBALTtay.
At,whay awn,dray anday alktay ofay eace?pay Iay atehay ethay ordway
Asay Iay atehay ell,hay allay Ontagues,may anday ee:thay
Avehay atay ee,thay owardcay.

Ey[_Thay ight._]fay

Enteray eethray oray ourfay Itizenscay ithway ubsclay.

IRSTfay ITIZENcay.
Ubs,clay illsbay anday artisans!pay Ike!stray Eatbay emthay own!day
Ownday ithway ethay Apulets!cay Ownday ithway ethay Ontagues!may

Enteray Apuletcay inay ishay own,gay anday Adylay Apuletcay.

APULETcay.
Atwhay oisenay isay is?thay Ivegay emay ymay onglay ord,sway o!hay

ADYlay APULETcay.
Aay utch,cray aay utch!cray Ywhay allcay youay orfay aay ord?sway

APULETcay.
Ymay ord,sway Iay ay!say Olday Ontaguemay isay ome,cay
Anday ourishesflay ishay adeblay inay itespay ofay emay.

Enteray Ontaguemay anday ishay Adylay Ontaguemay.

ONTAGUEmay.
Outhay illainvay Apulet!cay Oldhay emay ot,nay etlay emay ogay.

ADYlay ONTAGUEmay.
Outhay altshay otnay irstay oneay ootfay otay eeksay aay oefay.

Enteray Incepray Escalus,ay ithway Attendants.ay

INCEpRay.
Ebelliousray ubjects,say enemiesay otay eace,pay
Ofanerspray ofay isthay eighbour-stainednay eel,—stay
Illway eythay otnay ear?hay At,whay o!hay Youay en,may youay easts,bay
Atthay uenchqay ethay irefay ofay youray erniciouspay ageray
Ithway urplepay ountainsfay issuingay omfray youray eins,vay
Onay ainpay ofay orture,tay omfray osethay oodyblay andshay
Owthray youray istemper’dmay eaponsway otay ethay oundgray
Anday earhay ethay entencesay ofay youray ovedmay incepray.
Eethray ivilcay awls,bray edbray ofay anay airyay ord,way
Ybay ee,thay olday Apulet,cay anday Ontague,may
Avehay icethray isturb’dday ethay uietqay ofay ouray eets,stray
Anday ademay Erona’svay ancientay itizenscay
Astcay ybay eirthay avegray eseemingbay ornaments,ay
Otay ieldway olday artisans,pay inay andshay asay old,ay
Anker’dcay ithway eace,pay otay artpay youray anker’dcay atehay.
Ifay everay youay isturbday ouray eetsstray again,ay
Youray iveslay allshay aypay ethay orfeitfay ofay ethay eacepay.
Orfay isthay imetay allay ethay estray epartday away:ay
You,ay Apulet,cay allshay ogay alongay ithway e,may
Anday Ontague,may omecay youay isthay afternoon,ay
Otay owknay ouray artherfay easureplay inay isthay ase,cay
Otay olday Ee-town,fray ouray ommoncay udgement-placejay.
Onceay ore,may onay ainpay ofay eath,day allay enmay epartday.

Exeunt[_ay Incepray anday Attendants;ay Apulet,cay Adylay Apulet,cay Ybalt,tay
Itizenscay anday Ervants._]say

ONTAGUEmay.
Owhay etsay isthay ancientay uarrelqay ewnay abroach?ay
Eak,spay ephew,nay ereway youay ybay enwhay itay egan?bay

ENVOLIObay.
Erehay ereway ethay ervantssay ofay youray adversaryay
Anday yours,ay oseclay ightingfay ereay Iay idday approach.ay
Iay ewdray otay artpay em,thay inay ethay instantay amecay
Ethay ieryfay Ybalt,tay ithway ishay ordsway epar’d,pray
Ich,whay asay ehay eath’dbray efianceday otay ymay ears,ay
Ehay ungsway aboutay ishay ead,hay anday utcay ethay inds,way
Owhay othingnay urthay ithal,way iss’dhay imhay inay ornscay.
Ilewhay eway ereway interchangingay uststhray anday owsblay
Amecay oremay anday ore,may anday oughtfay onay artpay anday art,pay
Illtay ethay Incepray ame,cay owhay artedpay eitheray artpay.

ADYlay ONTAGUEmay.
Oay erewhay isay Omeo,ray awsay youay imhay oday?tay
Ightray adglay Iay amay ehay asway otnay atay isthay ayfray.

ENVOLIObay.
Adam,may anay ourhay eforebay ethay orshipp’dway unsay
Eer’dpay orthfay ethay oldengay indowway ofay ethay east,ay
Aay oubledtray indmay avedray emay otay alkway abroad,ay
Erewhay underneathay ethay ovegray ofay ycamoresay
Atthay estwardway ootethray omfray isthay itycay ide,say
Osay earlyay alkingway idday Iay eesay youray onsay.
Owardstay imhay Iay ade,may utbay ehay asway areway ofay e,may
Anday olestay intoay ethay overtcay ofay ethay oodway.
I,ay easuringmay ishay affectionsay ybay ymay own,ay
Ichwhay enthay ostmay oughtsay erewhay ostmay ightmay otnay ebay ound,fay
Eingbay oneay ootay anymay ybay ymay earyway elf,say
Ursu’dpay ymay umour,hay otnay ursuingpay is,hay
Anday adlyglay unn’dshay owhay adlyglay edflay omfray emay.

ONTAGUEmay.
Anymay aay orningmay athhay ehay erethay eenbay een,say
Ithway earstay augmentingay ethay eshfray orning’smay ew,day
Addingay otay oudsclay oremay oudsclay ithway ishay eepday ighs;say
Utbay allay osay oonsay asay ethay all-cheeringay unsay
Ouldshay inay ethay arthestfay eastay eginbay otay awdray
Ethay adyshay urtainscay omfray Aurora’say ed,bay
Awayay omfray ightlay ealsstay omehay ymay eavyhay on,say
Anday ivatepray inay ishay amberchay enspay imself,hay
Utsshay upay ishay indows,way ockslay airfay aylightday outay
Anday akesmay imselfhay anay artificialay ightnay.
Ackblay anday ortentouspay ustmay isthay umourhay ove,pray
Unlessay oodgay ounselcay aymay ethay ausecay emoveray.

ENVOLIObay.
Ymay oblenay uncle,ay oday youay owknay ethay ause?cay

ONTAGUEmay.
Iay eithernay owknay itay ornay ancay earnlay ofay imhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Avehay youay importun’day imhay ybay anyay eans?may

ONTAGUEmay.
Othbay ybay yselfmay anday anymay otheray iends;fray
Utbay e,hay ishay ownay affections’ay ounsellor,cay
Isay otay imself—Ihay illway otnay aysay owhay ue—tray
Utbay otay imselfhay osay ecretsay anday osay ose,clay
Osay arfay omfray oundingsay anday iscovery,day
Asay isay ethay udbay itbay ithway anay enviousay ormway
Ereay ehay ancay eadspray ishay eetsway eaveslay otay ethay air,ay
Oray edicateday ishay eautybay otay ethay unsay.
Ouldcay eway utbay earnlay omfray encewhay ishay orrowssay ow,gray
Eway ouldway asay illinglyway ivegay urecay asay owknay.

Enteray Omeoray.

ENVOLIObay.
Ee,say erewhay ehay omescay. Osay easeplay youay epstay aside;ay
I’llay owknay ishay ievancegray oray ebay uchmay eniedday.

ONTAGUEmay.
Iay ouldway outhay ertway osay appyhay ybay ythay aystay
Otay earhay uetray iftshray. Ome,cay adam,may et’slay away,ay

Exeunt[_ay Ontaguemay anday Adylay Ontague._]may

ENVOLIObay.
Oodgay orrow,may ousincay.

OMEOray.
Isay ethay ayday osay young?ay

ENVOLIObay.
Utbay ewnay uckstray inenay.

OMEOray.
Ayay e,may adsay ourshay eemsay onglay.
Asway atthay ymay atherfay atthay entway encehay osay ast?fay

ENVOLIObay.
Itay asway. Atwhay adnesssay engthenslay Omeo’sray ours?hay

OMEOray.
Otnay avinghay atthay ich,whay aving,hay akesmay emthay ortshay.

ENVOLIObay.
Inay ove?lay

OMEOray.
Out.ay

ENVOLIObay.
Ofay ove?lay

OMEOray.
Outay ofay erhay avourfay erewhay Iay amay inay ovelay.

ENVOLIObay.
Alasay atthay ovelay osay entlegay inay ishay iew,vay
Ouldshay ebay osay yrannoustay anday oughray inay oofpray.

OMEOray.
Alasay atthay ove,lay osewhay iewvay isay uffledmay ill,stay
Ould,shay ithoutway eyes,ay eesay athwayspay otay ishay ill!way
Erewhay allshay eway ine?day Oay e!may Atwhay ayfray asway ere?hay
Yetay elltay emay ot,nay orfay Iay avehay eardhay itay all.ay
Ere’shay uchmay otay oday ithway ate,hay utbay oremay ithway ove:lay
Y,whay en,thay Oay awlingbray ove!lay Oay ovinglay ate!hay
Oay anything,ay ofay othingnay irstfay eate!cray
Oay eavyhay ightness!lay erioussay anity!vay
Isshapenmay aoschay ofay ell-seemingway orms!fay
Eatherfay ofay ead,lay ightbray oke,smay oldcay ire,fay icksay ealth!hay
Ill-wakingstay eep,slay atthay isay otnay atwhay itay is!ay
Isthay ovelay eelfay I,ay atthay eelfay onay ovelay inay isthay.
Ostday outhay otnay augh?lay

ENVOLIObay.
Onay oz,cay Iay atherray eepway.

OMEOray.
Oodgay eart,hay atay at?whay

ENVOLIObay.
Atay ythay oodgay eart’shay oppression.ay

OMEOray.
Ywhay uchsay isay ove’slay ansgressiontray.
Iefsgray ofay inemay ownay ielay eavyhay inay ymay east,bray
Ichwhay outhay iltway opagatepray otay avehay itay estpray
Ithway oremay ofay inethay. Isthay ovelay atthay outhay asthay ownshay
Othday adday oremay iefgray otay ootay uchmay ofay inemay own.ay
Ovelay isay aay okesmay ademay ithway ethay umefay ofay ighs;say
Eingbay urg’d,pay aay irefay arklingspay inay overs’lay eyes;ay
Eingbay ex’d,vay aay easay ourish’dnay ithway overs’lay ears:tay
Atwhay isay itay else?ay Aay adnessmay ostmay iscreet,day
Aay okingchay all,gay anday aay eservingpray eetsway.
Arewell,fay ymay ozcay.

Oing._][_Gay

ENVOLIObay.
Oft!say Iay illway ogay along:ay
Anday ifay youay eavelay emay o,say youay oday emay ongwray.

OMEOray.
Ut!tay Iay avehay ostlay yself;may Iay amay otnay erehay.
Isthay isay otnay Omeo,ray e’shay omesay otheray erewhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Elltay emay inay adnesssay owhay isay atthay youay ove?lay

OMEOray.
At,whay allshay Iay oangray anday elltay ee?thay

ENVOLIObay.
Oan!gray Y,whay o;nay utbay adlysay elltay emay owhay.

OMEOray.
Idbay aay icksay anmay inay adnesssay akemay ishay ill,way
Aay ordway illay urg’day otay oneay atthay isay osay ill.ay
Inay adness,say ousin,cay Iay oday ovelay aay omanway.

ENVOLIObay.
Iay aim’day osay earnay enwhay Iay uppos’dsay youay ov’dlay.

OMEOray.
Aay ightray oodgay arkman,may anday e’sshay airfay Iay ovelay.

ENVOLIObay.
Aay ightray airfay ark,may airfay oz,cay isay oonestsay ithay.

OMEOray.
Ell,way inay atthay ithay youay iss:may e’llshay otnay ebay ithay
Ithway Upid’scay arrow,ay eshay athhay Ian’sday it;way
Anday inay ongstray oofpray ofay astitychay ellway arm’d,ay
Omfray ove’slay eakway ildishchay owbay eshay iveslay uncharm’d.ay
Eshay illway otnay aystay ethay iegesay ofay ovinglay ermstay
Ornay idebay encounterth’ay ofay assailingay eyes,ay
Ornay opeay erhay aplay otay aint-seducingsay old:gay
Oay e’sshay ichray inay eauty,bay onlyay oorpay
Atthay enwhay eshay ies,day ithway eautybay iesday erhay orestay.

ENVOLIObay.
Enthay eshay athhay ornsway atthay eshay illway illstay ivelay aste?chay

OMEOray.
Eshay ath,hay anday inay atthay aringspay akesmay ugehay aste;way
Orfay eautybay arv’dstay ithway erhay everity,say
Utscay eautybay offay omfray allay osteritypay.
Eshay isay ootay air,fay ootay ise;way iselyway ootay air,fay
Otay eritmay issblay ybay akingmay emay espairday.
Eshay athhay orswornfay otay ove,lay anday inay atthay owvay
Oday Iay ivelay ead,day atthay ivelay otay elltay itay ownay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ebay ul’dray ybay e,may orgetfay otay inkthay ofay erhay.

OMEOray.
Oay eachtay emay owhay Iay ouldshay orgetfay otay inkthay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ybay ivinggay ibertylay untoay inethay eyes;ay
Examineay otheray eautiesbay.

OMEOray.
Is’Tay ethay ayway
Otay allcay ers,hay exquisite,ay inay uestionqay oremay.
Esethay appyhay asksmay atthay isskay airfay adies’lay ows,bray
Eingbay ack,blay utspay usay inay indmay eythay idehay ethay air;fay
Ehay atthay isay uckenstray indblay annotcay orgetfay
Ethay eciouspray easuretray ofay ishay eyesightay ostlay.
Owshay emay aay istressmay atthay isay assingpay air,fay
Atwhay othday erhay eautybay ervesay utbay asay aay otenay
Erewhay Iay aymay eadray owhay ass’dpay atthay assingpay air?fay
Arewell,fay outhay anstcay otnay eachtay emay otay orgetfay.

ENVOLIObay.
I’llay aypay atthay octrine,day oray elseay ieday inay ebtday.

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay II.ay Aay Eetstray.

Enteray Apulet,cay Arispay anday Ervantsay.

APULETcay.
Utbay Ontaguemay isay oundbay asay ellway asay I,ay
Inay enaltypay alike;ay anday Is’tay otnay ard,hay Iay ink,thay
Orfay enmay osay olday asay eway otay eepkay ethay eacepay.

ARISpay.
Ofay onourablehay eckoningray areay youay oth,bay
Anday itypay Is’tay youay iv’dlay atay oddsay osay onglay.
Utbay ownay ymay ord,lay atwhay aysay youay otay ymay uit?say

APULETcay.
Utbay ayingsay o’eray atwhay Iay avehay aidsay eforebay.
Ymay ildchay isay yetay aay angerstray inay ethay orld,way
Eshay athhay otnay eensay ethay angechay ofay ourteenfay years;ay
Etlay otway oremay ummerssay itherway inay eirthay idepray
Ereay eway aymay inkthay erhay iperay otay ebay aay idebray.

ARISpay.
Youngeray anthay eshay areay appyhay othersmay ademay.

APULETcay.
Anday ootay oonsay arr’dmay areay osethay osay earlyay ademay.
Ethay earthay athhay allowedsway allay ymay opeshay utbay e,shay
Eshay isay ethay opefulhay adylay ofay ymay earth:ay
Utbay ooway er,hay entlegay Aris,pay etgay erhay eart,hay
Ymay illway otay erhay onsentcay isay utbay aay art;pay
Anday eshay agree,ay ithinway erhay opescay ofay oicechay
Ieslay ymay onsentcay anday airfay accordingay oicevay.
Isthay ightnay Iay oldhay anay olday accustom’day east,fay
Eretowhay Iay avehay inviteday anymay aay uest,gay
Uchsay asay Iay ove,lay anday youay amongay ethay ore,stay
Oneay ore,may ostmay elcome,way akesmay ymay umbernay oremay.
Atay ymay oorpay ousehay ooklay otay eholdbay isthay ightnay
Earth-treadingay arsstay atthay akemay arkday eavenhay ight:lay
Uchsay omfortcay asay oday ustylay youngay enmay eelfay
Enwhay ellway apparell’day Aprilay onay ethay eelhay
Ofay impinglay interway eads,tray evenay uchsay elightday
Amongay eshfray emalefay udsbay allshay youay isthay ightnay
Inheritay atay ymay ousehay. Earhay all,ay allay ee,say
Anday ikelay erhay ostmay osewhay eritmay ostmay allshay e:bay
Ich,whay onay oremay iewvay ofay any,may ine,may eingbay one,ay
Aymay andstay inay umber,nay oughthay inay eckoningray onenay.
Ome,cay ogay ithway emay. O,gay irrah,say udgetray aboutay
Oughthray airfay Erona;vay indfay osethay ersonspay outay
Osewhay amesnay areay ittenwray ere,thay Ives[_gay aay aper_]pay anday otay emthay ay,say
Ymay ousehay anday elcomeway onay eirthay easureplay aystay.

Exeunt[_ay Apuletcay anday Aris._]pay

ERVANTsay.
Indfay emthay outay osewhay amesnay areay ittenwray ere!hay Itay isay ittenwray atthay ethay
oemakershay ouldshay eddlemay ithway ishay yarday anday ethay ailortay ithway ishay ast,lay ethay
isherfay ithway ishay encil,pay anday ethay ainterpay ithway ishay ets;nay utbay Iay amay entsay otay
indfay osethay ersonspay osewhay amesnay areay erehay it,wray anday ancay evernay indfay atwhay
amesnay ethay itingwray ersonpay athhay erehay itwray. Iay ustmay otay ethay earnedlay. Inay oodgay
ime!tay

Enteray Envoliobay anday Omeoray.

ENVOLIObay.
Ut,tay an,may oneay irefay urnsbay outay another’say urning,bay
Oneay ainpay isay essen’dlay ybay another’say anguish;ay
Urntay iddy,gay anday ebay olphay ybay ackwardbay urning;tay
Oneay esperateday iefgray urescay ithway another’say anguish:lay
Aketay outhay omesay ewnay infectionay otay ythay eye,ay
Anday ethay ankray oisonpay ofay ethay olday illway ieday.

OMEOray.
Youray antainplay eaflay isay excellentay orfay atthay.

ENVOLIObay.
Orfay at,whay Iay aypray ee?thay

OMEOray.
Orfay youray okenbray inshay.

ENVOLIObay.
Y,whay Omeo,ray artay outhay ad?may

OMEOray.
Otnay ad,may utbay oundbay oremay anthay aay admanmay is:ay
Utshay upay inay ison,pray eptkay ithoutway ymay ood,fay
Ipp’dwhay anday ormentedtay and—God-den,ay oodgay ellowfay.

ERVANTsay.
Odgay i’gay o-dengay. Iay ay,pray ir,say ancay youay ead?ray

OMEOray.
Ay,ay inemay ownay ortunefay inay ymay iserymay.

ERVANTsay.
Erhapspay youay avehay earnedlay itay ithoutway ookbay.
Utbay Iay ay,pray ancay youay eadray anythingay youay ee?say

OMEOray.
Ay,ay Ifay Iay owknay ethay etterslay anday ethay anguagelay.

ERVANTsay.
Yeay aysay onestly,hay estray youay erry!may

OMEOray.
Ay,stay ellow;fay Iay ancay eadray.

E[_Hay eadsray ethay etter._]lay

Ignior_Say Artinomay anday ishay ifeway anday aughters;day
Ountycay Anselmoay anday ishay eauteousbay isters;say
Ethay adylay idowway ofay Utruvio;ay
Igniorsay Acentioplay anday ishay ovelylay ieces;nay

Up.ay

OMEOray.
Itherwhay otay upper?say

ERVANTsay.
Otay ouray ousehay.

OMEOray.
Osewhay ouse?hay

Ymay aster’smay.

anday ifay youay ebay otnay ofay ethay ousehay ofay Ontagues,may Iay aypray omecay anday ushcray aay
upcay ofay ineway. Estray youay errymay.

Exit._][_ay

ENVOLIObay.
Atay isthay amesay ancientay eastfay ofay Apulet’scay
Upssay ethay airfay Osalineray omwhay outhay osay ov’st;lay
Ithway allay ethay admireday eautiesbay ofay Eronavay.
Ogay itherthay anday ithway unattainteday eye,ay
Omparecay erhay acefay ithway omesay atthay Iay allshay ow,shay
Anday Iay illway akemay eethay inkthay ythay answay aay owcray.

OMEOray.
Enwhay ethay evoutday eligionray ofay inemay eyeay
Aintainsmay uchsay alsehood,fay enthay urntay earstay otay ire;fay
Anday esethay o,whay oftenay own’d,dray ouldcay evernay ie,day
Ansparenttray eretics,hay ebay urntbay orfay iarslay.
Oneay airerfay anthay ymay ove?lay Ethay all-seeingay unsay
E’ernay awsay erhay atchmay incesay irstfay ethay orldway egunbay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ut,tay youay awsay erhay air,fay onenay elseay eingbay y,bay
Erselfhay ois’dpay ithway erselfhay inay eitheray eye:ay
Utbay inay atthay ystalcray alesscay etlay erethay ebay eigh’dway
Youray ady’slay ovelay againstay omesay otheray aidmay
Atthay Iay illway owshay youay iningshay atay isthay east,fay
Anday eshay allshay antscay owshay ellway atthay ownay owsshay estbay.

OMEOray.
I’llay ogay along,ay onay uchsay ightsay otay ebay own,shay
Utbay otay ejoiceray inay endoursplay ofay ymay own.ay

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay III.ay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

Enteray Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Urse,nay ere’swhay ymay aughter?day Allcay erhay orthfay otay emay.

URSEnay.
Ow,nay ybay ymay aidenhead,may atay elvetway yearay old,ay
Iay adebay erhay omecay. At,whay amb!lay Atwhay adybird!lay
Odgay orbid!fay Ere’swhay isthay irl?gay At,whay Uliet!jay

Enteray Ulietjay.

ULIETjay.
Owhay ow,nay owhay alls?cay

URSEnay.
Youray othermay.

ULIETjay.
Adam,may Iay amay erehay. Atwhay isay youray ill?way

ADYlay APULETcay.
Isthay isay ethay attermay. Urse,nay ivegay eavelay awhile,ay
Eway ustmay alktay inay ecretsay. Urse,nay omecay ackbay again,ay
Iay avehay emember’dray e,may ou’sthay earhay ouray ounselcay.
Outhay owestknay ymay aughter’sday ofay aay ettypray age.ay

URSEnay.
Aith,fay Iay ancay elltay erhay ageay untoay anay ourhay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
E’sshay otnay ourteenfay.

URSEnay.
I’llay aylay ourteenfay ofay ymay eeth,tay
Anday yet,ay otay ymay eentay ebay itay oken,spay Iay avehay utbay our,fay
Eshay isay otnay ourteenfay. Owhay onglay isay itay ownay
Otay Ammas-tide?lay

ADYlay APULETcay.
Aay ortnightfay anday odday aysday.

URSEnay.
Evenay oray odd,ay ofay allay aysday inay ethay year,ay
Omecay Ammaslay Eveay atay ightnay allshay eshay ebay ourteenfay.
Usansay anday e,—Godshay estray allay Istianchray ouls!—say
Ereway ofay anay age.ay Ell,way Usansay isay ithway Od;gay
Eshay asway ootay oodgay orfay emay. Utbay asay Iay aid,say
Onay Ammaslay Eveay atay ightnay allshay eshay ebay ourteen;fay
Atthay allshay e,shay arry;may Iay ememberray itay ellway.
Is’Tay incesay ethay earthquakeay ownay elevenay years;ay
Anday eshay asway ean’d,—Iway evernay allshay orgetfay it—,ay
Ofay allay ethay aysday ofay ethay year,ay uponay atthay ay:day
Orfay Iay adhay enthay aidlay ormwoodway otay ymay ug,day
Ittingsay inay ethay unsay underay ethay ovehouseday all;way
Ymay ordlay anday youay ereway enthay atay Antua:may
Ay,nay Iay oday earbay aay ainbray. Utbay asay Iay aid,say
Enwhay itay idday astetay ethay ormwoodway onay ethay ipplenay
Ofay ymay ugday anday eltfay itay itter,bay ettypray ool,fay
Otay eesay itay etchy,tay anday allfay outay ithway ethay ug!day
Ake,shay uothqay ethay ovehouse:day As’tway onay eed,nay Iay ow,tray
Otay idbay emay udgetray.
Anday incesay atthay imetay itay isay elevenay years;ay
Orfay enthay eshay ouldcay andstay alone;ay ay,nay ybay oodth’ray
Eshay ouldcay avehay unray anday addledway allay about;ay
Orfay evenay ethay ayday eforebay eshay okebray erhay ow,bray
Anday enthay ymay usband,—Godhay ebay ithway ishay oul!say
Aay asway aay errymay an,—tookmay upay ethay ild:chay
Yea,’‘ay uothqay e,hay Ost‘day outhay allfay uponay ythay ace?fay
Outhay iltway allfay ackwardbay enwhay outhay asthay oremay it;way
Iltway outhay ot,nay Ule?’jay and,ay ybay ymay olidame,hay
Ethay ettypray etchwray eftlay ying,cray anday aidsay Ay’‘ay.
Otay eesay ownay owhay aay estjay allshay omecay about.ay
Iay arrant,way anday Iay ouldshay ivelay aay ousandthay years,ay
Iay evernay ouldshay orgetfay it.ay Ilt‘Way outhay ot,nay Ule?’jay uothqay e;hay
And,ay ettypray ool,fay itay inted,stay anday aidsay Ay.’‘ay

ADYlay APULETcay.
Enoughay ofay is;thay Iay aypray eethay oldhay ythay eacepay.

URSEnay.
Yes,ay adam,may yetay Iay annotcay oosechay utbay augh,lay
Otay inkthay itay ouldshay eavelay ying,cray anday aysay Ay’;‘ay
Anday yetay Iay arrantway itay adhay uponay itay owbray
Aay umpbay asay igbay asay aay youngay ockerel’scay one;stay
Aay erilouspay ock,knay anday itay iedcray itterlybay.
Yea,’‘ay uothqay ymay usband,hay All’st‘fay uponay ythay ace?fay
Outhay iltway allfay ackwardbay enwhay outhay omestcay otay age;ay
Iltway outhay ot,nay Ule?’jay itay inted,stay anday aidsay Ay’‘ay.

ULIETjay.
Anday intstay outhay oo,tay Iay aypray ee,thay Urse,nay aysay I.ay

URSEnay.
Eace,pay Iay avehay oneday. Odgay arkmay eethay otay ishay acegray
Outhay astway ethay ettiestpray abebay atthay e’eray Iay urs’d:nay
Anday Iay ightmay ivelay otay eesay eethay arriedmay once,ay Iay avehay ymay ishway.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Arry,may atthay arrymay isay ethay eryvay emethay
Iay amecay otay alktay of.ay Elltay e,may aughterday Uliet,jay
Owhay andsstay youray ispositionday otay ebay arried?may

ULIETjay.
Itay isay anay onourhay atthay Iay eamdray otnay of.ay

URSEnay.
Anay onour!hay Ereway otnay Iay inethay onlyay urse,nay
Iay ouldway aysay outhay adsthay uck’dsay isdomway omfray ythay eattay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Ell,way inkthay ofay arriagemay ow:nay youngeray anthay you,ay
Erehay inay Erona,vay adieslay ofay esteem,ay
Areay ademay alreadyay othersmay. Ybay ymay ountcay
Iay asway youray othermay uchmay uponay esethay yearsay
Atthay youay areay ownay aay aidmay. Us,thay en,thay inay ief;bray
Ethay aliantvay Arispay eekssay youay orfay ishay ovelay.

URSEnay.
Aay an,may youngay ady!lay Ady,lay uchsay aay anmay
Asay allay ethay orld—whyway e’shay aay anmay ofay axway.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Erona’svay ummersay athhay otnay uchsay aay owerflay.

URSEnay.
Ay,nay e’shay aay ower,flay inay aithfay aay eryvay owerflay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Atwhay aysay you,ay ancay youay ovelay ethay entleman?gay
Isthay ightnay youay allshay eholdbay imhay atay ouray east;fay
Eadray o’eray ethay olumevay ofay youngay Aris’pay ace,fay
Anday indfay elightday itwray erethay ithway eauty’sbay enpay.
Examineay everyay arriedmay ineament,lay
Anday eesay owhay oneay anotheray endslay ontent;cay
Anday atwhay obscur’day inay isthay airfay olumevay ies,lay
Indfay ittenwray inay ethay argentmay ofay ishay eyes.ay
Isthay eciouspray ookbay ofay ove,lay isthay unbounday over,lay
Otay eautifybay im,hay onlyay ackslay aay over:cay
Ethay ishfay iveslay inay ethay ea;say anday Is’tay uchmay idepray
Orfay airfay ithoutway ethay airfay ithinway otay idehay.
Atthay ookbay inay any’smay eyesay othday areshay ethay ory,glay
Atthay inay oldgay aspsclay ockslay inay ethay oldengay ory;stay
Osay allshay youay areshay allay atthay ehay othday ossess,pay
Ybay avinghay im,hay akingmay yourselfay onay esslay.

URSEnay.
Onay ess,lay aynay iggerbay. Omenway owgray ybay enmay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Eakspay iefly,bray ancay youay ikelay ofay Aris’pay ove?lay

ULIETjay.
I’llay ooklay otay ike,lay ifay ookinglay ikinglay ove:may
Utbay onay oremay eepday illway Iay endartay inemay eyeay
Anthay youray onsentcay ivesgay engthstray otay akemay itay yflay.

Enteray aay Ervantsay.

ERVANTsay.
Adam,may ethay uestsgay areay ome,cay uppersay ervedsay up,ay youay alled,cay ymay youngay adylay
askeday or,fay ethay Ursenay ursedcay inay ethay antry,pay anday everythingay inay extremity.ay
Iay ustmay encehay otay ait,way Iay eseechbay youay ollowfay aightstray.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Eway ollowfay eethay.

Exit[_ay Ervant._]say

Uliet,jay ethay Ountycay aysstay.

URSEnay.
O,gay irl,gay eeksay appyhay ightsnay otay appyhay aysday.

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay IV.ay Aay Eetstray.

Enteray Omeo,ray Ercutio,may Envolio,bay ithway ivefay oray ixsay Askers;may
Orch-bearerstay anday others.ay

OMEOray.
At,whay allshay isthay eechspay ebay okespay orfay ouray excuse?ay
Oray allshay eway onay ithoutway apology?ay

ENVOLIObay.
Ethay ateday isay outay ofay uchsay olixity:pray
E’llway avehay onay Upidcay oodwink’dhay ithway aay arf,scay
Earingbay aay Artar’stay aintedpay owbay ofay ath,lay
Aringscay ethay adieslay ikelay aay ow-keeper;cray
Ornay onay ithout-bookway ologue,pray aintlyfay okespay
Afteray ethay ompter,pray orfay ouray entrance:ay
Utbay etlay emthay easuremay usay ybay atwhay eythay ill,way
E’llway easuremay emthay aay easure,may anday ebay onegay.

OMEOray.
Ivegay emay aay orch,tay Iay amay otnay orfay isthay ambling;ay
Eingbay utbay eavyhay Iay illway earbay ethay ightlay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ay,nay entlegay Omeo,ray eway ustmay avehay youay anceday.

OMEOray.
Otnay I,ay elievebay e,may youay avehay ancingday oes,shay
Ithway imblenay oles,say Iay avehay aay oulsay ofay eadlay
Osay akesstay emay otay ethay oundgray Iay annotcay ovemay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Youay areay aay over,lay orrowbay Upid’scay ings,way
Anday oarsay ithway emthay aboveay aay ommoncay oundbay.

OMEOray.
Iay amay ootay oresay enpierceday ithway ishay aftshay
Otay oarsay ithway ishay ightlay eathers,fay anday osay ound,bay
Iay annotcay oundbay aay itchpay aboveay ullday oeway.
Underay ove’slay eavyhay urdenbay oday Iay inksay.

ERCUTIOmay.
And,ay otay inksay inay it,ay ouldshay youay urdenbay ove;lay
Ootay eatgray oppressionay orfay aay endertay ingthay.

OMEOray.
Isay ovelay aay endertay ing?thay Itay isay ootay ough,ray
Ootay ude,ray ootay oisterous;bay anday itay ickspray ikelay ornthay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ifay ovelay ebay oughray ithway you,ay ebay oughray ithway ove;lay
Ickpray ovelay orfay icking,pray anday youay eatbay ovelay ownday.
Ivegay emay aay asecay otay utpay ymay isagevay in:ay Utting[_Pay onay aay ask._]may
Aay isorvay orfay aay isorvay. Atwhay arecay Iay
Atwhay uriouscay eyeay othday uoteqay eformities?day
Erehay areay ethay eetle-browsbay allshay ushblay orfay emay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ome,cay ockknay anday enter;ay anday onay oonersay inay
Utbay everyay anmay etakebay imhay otay ishay egslay.

OMEOray.
Aay orchtay orfay e:may etlay antons,way ightlay ofay eart,hay
Ickletay ethay enselesssay ushesray ithway eirthay eels;hay
Orfay Iay amay overb’dpray ithway aay andsiregray ase,phray
I’llay ebay aay andle-holdercay anday ooklay on,ay
Ethay amegay asway e’ernay osay air,fay anday Iay amay oneday.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ut,tay un’sday ethay ouse,may ethay onstable’scay ownay ord:way
Ifay outhay artay un,day e’llway awdray eethay omfray ethay iremay
Oray avesay youray everenceray ove,lay ereinwhay outhay ickeststay
Upay otay ethay ears.ay Ome,cay eway urnbay aylight,day ohay.

OMEOray.
Ay,nay at’sthay otnay osay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Iay eanmay ir,say inay elayday
Eway asteway ouray ightslay inay ain,vay ightlay ightslay ybay ayday.
Aketay ouray oodgay eaning,may orfay ouray udgmentjay itssay
Ivefay imestay inay atthay ereay onceay inay ouray ivefay itsway.

OMEOray.
Anday eway eanmay ellway inay oinggay otay isthay ask;may
Utbay Is’tay onay itway otay ogay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Y,whay aymay oneay ask?ay

OMEOray.
Iay eamtdray aay eamdray onighttay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Anday osay idday I.ay

OMEOray.
Ellway atwhay asway yours?ay

ERCUTIOmay.
Atthay eamersdray oftenay ielay.

OMEOray.
Inay edbay asleep,ay ilewhay eythay oday eamdray ingsthay uetray.

ERCUTIOmay.
O,ay en,thay Iay eesay Ueenqay Abmay athhay eenbay ithway you.ay
Eshay isay ethay airies’fay idwife,may anday eshay omescay
Inay apeshay onay iggerbay anthay anay agate-stoneay
Onay ethay ore-fingerfay ofay anay alderman,ay
Awndray ithway aay eamtay ofay ittlelay atomiesay
Overay en’smay osesnay asay eythay ielay asleep:ay
Erhay aggon-spokesway ademay ofay onglay inners’spay egs;lay
Ethay over,cay ofay ethay ingsway ofay asshoppers;gray
Erhay aces,tray ofay ethay allestsmay ider’sspay eb;way
Ethay ollars,cay ofay ethay oonshine’smay ateryway eams;bay
Erhay ipwhay ofay icket’scray one;bay ethay ash,lay ofay ilm;fay
Erhay aggoner,way aay allsmay ey-coatedgray at,gnay
Otnay alfhay osay igbay asay aay oundray ittlelay ormway
Ick’dpray omfray ethay azylay ingerfay ofay aay aid:may
Erhay ariotchay isay anay emptyay azelnut,hay
Ademay ybay ethay oinerjay uirrelsqay oray olday ub,gray
Imetay outay o’ay indmay ethay airies’fay oachmakerscay.
Anday inay isthay atestay eshay allopsgay ightnay ybay ightnay
Oughthray overs’lay ains,bray anday enthay eythay eamdray ofay ove;lay
O’eray ourtiers’cay ees,knay atthay eamdray onay urtsiescay aight;stray
O’eray awyers’lay ingers,fay owhay aightstray eamdray onay ees;fay
O’eray adies’lay ips,lay owhay aightstray onay isseskay eam,dray
Ichwhay oftay ethay angryay Abmay ithway istersblay agues,play
Ecausebay eirthay eathsbray ithway eetmeatssway aintedtay are:ay
Ometimesay eshay allopsgay o’eray aay ourtier’scay ose,nay
Anday enthay eamsdray ehay ofay ellingsmay outay aay uit;say
Anday ometimesay omescay eshay ithway aay ithe-pig’stay ail,tay
Icklingtay aay arson’spay osenay asay aay ieslay asleep,ay
Enthay eamsdray ehay ofay anotheray enefice:bay
Ometimesay eshay ivethdray o’eray aay oldier’ssay eck,nay
Anday enthay eamsdray ehay ofay uttingcay oreignfay oats,thray
Ofay eaches,bray ambuscados,ay Anishspay ades,blay
Ofay ealthshay ivefay athomfay eep;day anday enthay anonay
Umsdray inay ishay ear,ay atay ichwhay ehay artsstay anday akes;way
And,ay eingbay usthay ighted,fray earssway aay ayerpray oray o,tway
Anday eepsslay again.ay Isthay isay atthay eryvay Abmay
Atthay atsplay ethay anesmay ofay orseshay inay ethay ight;nay
Anday akesbay ethay elf-locksay inay oulfay uttishslay airs,hay
Ich,whay onceay untangled,ay uchmay isfortunemay odes:bay
Isthay isay ethay ag,hay enwhay aidsmay ielay onay eirthay acks,bay
Atthay essespray em,thay anday earnslay emthay irstfay otay ear,bay
Akingmay emthay omenway ofay oodgay arriage:cay
Isthay isay e,—shay

OMEOray.
Eace,pay eace,pay Ercutio,may eace,pay
Outhay alk’sttay ofay othingnay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ue,tray Iay alktay ofay eams,dray
Ichwhay areay ethay ildrenchay ofay anay idleay ain,bray
Egotbay ofay othingnay utbay ainvay antasy,fay
Ichwhay isay asay inthay ofay ubstancesay asay ethay air,ay
Anday oremay inconstantay anthay ethay ind,way owhay oosway
Evenay ownay ethay ozenfray osombay ofay ethay orth,nay
And,ay eingbay anger’d,ay uffspay awayay omfray ence,thay
Urningtay ishay idesay otay ethay ew-droppingday outhsay.

ENVOLIObay.
Isthay indway youay alktay ofay owsblay usay omfray ourselves:ay
Uppersay isay one,day anday eway allshay omecay ootay atelay.

OMEOray.
Iay earfay ootay early:ay orfay ymay indmay isgivesmay
Omesay onsequencecay yetay anginghay inay ethay ars,stay
Allshay itterlybay eginbay ishay earfulfay ateday
Ithway isthay ight’snay evels;ray anday expireay ethay ermtay

Irectday ymay uitsay. On,ay ustylay entlemen!gay

ENVOLIObay.
Ike,stray umdray.

YBALTtay.

APULETcay.

ACTay IIay


Enteray Oruschay.

ORUScHay.
Ownay olday esireday othday inay ishay eathbedday ie,lay
Anday youngay affectionay apesgay otay ebay ishay eir;hay
Atthay airfay orfay ichwhay ovelay oan’dgray orfay anday ouldway ie,day
Ithway endertay Ulietjay atch’d,may isay ownay otnay airfay.
Ownay Omeoray isay elov’d,bay anday oveslay again,ay
Alikeay ewitchedbay ybay ethay armchay ofay ooks;lay
Utbay otay ishay oefay uppos’dsay ehay ustmay omplain,cay
Anday eshay ealstay ove’slay eetsway aitbay omfray earfulfay ooks:hay
Eingbay eldhay aay oe,fay ehay aymay otnay avehay accessay
Otay eathebray uchsay owsvay asay overslay useay otay ear;sway
Anday eshay asay uchmay inay ove,lay erhay eansmay uchmay esslay
Otay eetmay erhay ewnay elovedbay anywhere.ay
Utbay assionpay endslay emthay ower,pay imetay eans,may otay eet,may
Emperingtay extremitiesay ithway extremeay eetsway.

Exit._][_ay

ENEsCay I.ay Anay openay aceplay adjoiningay Apulet’scay Ardengay.

ENVOLIObay.
Omeo!ray Ymay ousincay Omeo!ray Omeo!ray

ERCUTIOmay.
Ehay isay ise,way

Ay,nay I’llay onjurecay ootay.
Omeo!ray Umours!hay Adman!may Assion!pay Over!lay
Appearay outhay inay ethay ikenesslay ofay aay igh,say
Eakspay utbay oneay yme,rhay anday Iay amay atisfied;say
Ycray utbay Ah‘ay e!’may Onouncepray utbay Ovelay anday ove;day
Eakspay otay ymay ossipgay Enusvay oneay airfay ord,way
Oneay icknamenay orfay erhay urblindpay onsay anday eir,hay
Youngay Abrahamay Upid,cay ehay atthay otshay osay imtray
Enwhay Ingkay Ophetuacay ov’dlay ethay eggar-maidbay.

Ybay erhay ighhay oreheadfay anday erhay arletscay ip,lay
Ybay erhay inefay oot,fay aightstray eg,lay anday uiveringqay igh,thay
Anday ethay emesnesday atthay erethay adjacentay ie,lay
Atthay inay ythay ikenesslay outhay appearay otay us.ay

ENVOLIObay.
Anay ifay ehay earhay ee,thay outhay iltway angeray imhay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Isthay annotcay angeray imhay. Ould’Tway angeray imhay

Ofay omesay angestray ature,nay ettinglay itay erethay andstay
Illtay eshay adhay aidlay it,ay anday onjur’dcay itay own;day
Atthay ereway omesay itespay. Ymay invocationay
Isay airfay anday onest,hay and,ay inay ishay istress’may ame,nay
Iay onjurecay onlyay utbay otay aiseray upay imhay.

ENVOLIObay.
Ome,cay ehay athhay idhay imselfhay amongay esethay eestray
Otay ebay onsortedcay ithway ethay umoroushay ightnay.
Indblay isay ishay ove,lay anday estbay efitsbay ethay arkday.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ifay ovelay ebay ind,blay ovelay annotcay ithay ethay arkmay.
Ownay illway ehay itsay underay aay edlarmay ee,tray
Anday ishway ishay istressmay ereway atthay indkay ofay uitfray
Asay aidsmay allcay edlarsmay enwhay eythay aughlay alone.ay
Oay Omeo,ray atthay eshay ere,way Oay atthay eshay ereway
Anay open-arseay anday outhay aay operinpay ear!pay
Omeo,ray oodgay ightnay. I’llay otay ymay uckle-bedtray.
Isthay ield-bedfay isay ootay oldcay orfay emay otay eepslay.
Ome,cay allshay eway o?gay

ENVOLIObay.
Ogay en;thay orfay Is’tay inay ainvay
Otay eeksay imhay erehay atthay eansmay otnay otay ebay oundfay.

ENEsCay II.ay Apulet’scay Ardengay.

Enteray Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Ehay estsjay atay arsscay atthay evernay eltfay aay oundway.

Ulietjay appearsay aboveay atay aay indowway.

Utbay oft,say atwhay ightlay oughthray yonderay indowway eaks?bray
Itay isay ethay east,ay anday Ulietjay isay ethay un!say
Ariseay airfay unsay anday illkay ethay enviousay oon,may
Owhay isay alreadyay icksay anday alepay ithway ief,gray
Atthay outhay erhay aidmay artay arfay oremay airfay anthay eshay.
Ebay otnay erhay aidmay incesay eshay isay envious;ay
Erhay estalvay iverylay isay utbay icksay anday een,gray
Anday onenay utbay oolsfay oday earway it;ay astcay itay off.ay
Itay isay ymay ady,lay Oay itay isay ymay ove!lay
O,ay atthay eshay ewknay eshay ere!way
Eshay eaks,spay yetay eshay ayssay othingnay. Atwhay ofay at?thay
Erhay eyeay iscourses,day Iay illway answeray it.ay
Iay amay ootay old,bay Is’tay otnay otay emay eshay eaksspay.
Otway ofay ethay airestfay arsstay inay allay ethay eaven,hay
Avinghay omesay usiness,bay oday entreatay erhay eyesay
Otay inkletway inay eirthay eressphay illtay eythay eturnray.
Atwhay ifay erhay eyesay ereway ere,thay eythay inay erhay ead?hay
Ethay ightnessbray ofay erhay eekchay ouldway ameshay osethay ars,stay
Asay aylightday othday aay amp;lay erhay eyesay inay eavenhay
Ouldway oughthray ethay airyay egionray eamstray osay ightbray
Atthay irdsbay ouldway ingsay anday inkthay itay ereway otnay ightnay.
Eesay owhay eshay eanslay erhay eekchay uponay erhay andhay.
Oay atthay Iay ereway aay oveglay uponay atthay and,hay
Atthay Iay ightmay ouchtay atthay eekchay.

ULIETjay.
Ayay emay.

OMEOray.
Eshay eaksspay.
Oay eakspay againay ightbray angel,ay orfay outhay artay
Asay oriousglay otay isthay ight,nay eingbay o’eray ymay ead,hay

Elongingbay otay aay anmay. Oay ebay omesay otheray amenay.
At’swhay inay aay ame?nay Atthay ichwhay eway allcay aay oseray

ENEsCay III.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.

Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay ithway aay asketbay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Ethay ey-ey’dgray ornmay ilessmay onay ethay owningfray ight,nay
Equeringchay ethay easternay oudsclay ithway eaksstray ofay ight;lay
Anday eckledflay arknessday ikelay aay unkarddray eelsray
Omfray orthfay ay’sday athway,pay ademay ybay Itan’stay ieryfay eelswhay
Ow,nay ereay ethay unsay advanceay ishay urningbay eye,ay
Ethay ayday otay eer,chay anday ight’snay ankday ewday otay y,dray
Iay ustmay upfillay isthay osieray agecay ofay oursay
Ithway alefulbay eedsway anday ecious-juicedpray owersflay.
Ethay earthay at’sthay ature’snay other,may isay erhay omb;tay
Atwhay isay erhay uryingbay ave,gray atthay isay erhay omb:way
Anday omfray erhay ombway ildrenchay ofay iversday indkay
Eway uckingsay onay erhay aturalnay osombay indfay.
Anymay orfay anymay irtuesvay excellent,ay
Onenay utbay orfay ome,say anday yetay allay ifferentday.
O,ay icklemay isay ethay owerfulpay acegray atthay ieslay
Inay ants,play erbs,hay ones,stay anday eirthay uetray ualitiesqay.
Orfay aughtnay osay ilevay atthay onay ethay earthay othday ivelay
Utbay otay ethay earthay omesay ecialspay oodgay othday ive;gay
Ornay aughtay osay oodgay ut,bay ain’dstray omfray atthay airfay use,ay
Evoltsray omfray uetray irth,bay umblingstay onay abuse.ay
Irtuevay itselfay urnstay icevay eingbay isapplied,may
Anday icevay ometime’ssay ybay actionay ignifiedday.

Enteray Omeoray.

Ithinway ethay infantay indray ofay isthay eakway owerflay

Orfay is,thay eingbay elt,smay ithway atthay artpay eerschay eachay art;pay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Enedicite!bay
Atwhay earlyay onguetay osay eetsway alutethsay e?may

ethay immortalay assado,pay ethay untopay everso,ray ethay ayhay.

ULIETjay.

Anday ereforethay athhay ethay ind-swiftway Upidcay ingsway.
Ownay isay ethay unsay uponay ethay ighmosthay illhay

Ah,ay Uliet,jay ifay ethay easuremay ofay ythay oyjay
Ebay eap’dhay ikelay ine,may anday atthay ythay illskay ebay oremay
Otay azonblay it,ay enthay eetensway ithway ythay eathbray
Isthay eighbournay air,ay anday etlay ichray usic’smay onguetay
Unfolday ethay imagin’day appinesshay atthay othbay
Eceiveray inay eitheray ybay isthay earday encounter.ay

ULIETjay.
Onceitcay oremay ichray inay attermay anthay inay ords,way
Agsbray ofay ishay ubstance,say otnay ofay ornament.ay
Eythay areay utbay eggarsbay atthay ancay ountcay eirthay orth;way
Utbay ymay uetray ovelay isay owngray otay uchsay excess,ay
Iay annotcay umsay upay umsay ofay alfhay ymay ealthway.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Ome,cay omecay ithway e,may anday eway illway akemay ortshay ork,way
Or,fay ybay youray eaves,lay youay allshay otnay aystay aloneay
Illtay olyhay urchchay incorporateay otway inay one.ay

Exeunt._][_ay




ACTay IIIay

ENEsCay I.ay Aay ublicpay Aceplay.


Enteray Ercutio,may Envolio,bay Agepay anday Ervantssay.

ENVOLIObay.
Iay aypray ee,thay oodgay Ercutio,may et’slay etire:ray
Ethay ayday isay ot,hay ethay Apuletscay abroad,ay
Anday ifay eway eet,may eway allshay otnay apescay aay awl,bray
Orfay ownay esethay othay ays,day isay ethay admay oodblay irringstay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Outhay artay ikelay oneay ofay esethay ellowsfay at,thay enwhay ehay entersay ethay onfinescay ofay
aay avern,tay apsclay emay ishay ordsway uponay ethay able,tay anday ayssay Od‘Gay endsay emay onay
eednay ofay ee!’thay anday ybay ethay operationay ofay ethay econdsay upcay awsdray imhay onay ethay
awer,dray enwhay indeeday erethay isay onay eednay.

ENVOLIObay.
Amay Iay ikelay uchsay aay ellow?fay

ERCUTIOmay.
Ome,cay ome,cay outhay artay asay othay aay Ackjay inay ythay oodmay asay anyay inay Italy;ay anday asay
oonsay ovedmay otay ebay oody,may anday asay oonsay oodymay otay ebay ovedmay.

ENVOLIObay.
Anday atwhay o?tay

ERCUTIOmay.
Ay,nay anay erethay ereway otway uch,say eway ouldshay avehay onenay ortly,shay orfay oneay ouldway
illkay ethay other.ay Ou?thay Y,whay outhay iltway uarrelqay ithway aay anmay atthay athhay aay
airhay oremay oray aay airhay esslay inay ishay eardbay anthay outhay asthay. Outhay iltway uarrelqay
ithway aay anmay orfay ackingcray uts,nay avinghay onay otheray easonray utbay ecausebay outhay
asthay azelhay eyes.ay Atwhay eyeay utbay uchsay anay eyeay ouldway yspay outay uchsay aay uarrel?qay
Ythay eadhay isay asay ullfay ofay uarrelsqay asay anay eggay isay ullfay ofay eat,may anday yetay ythay
eadhay athhay eenbay eatenbay asay addleay asay anay eggay orfay uarrellingqay. Outhay asthay
uarrelledqay ithway aay anmay orfay oughingcay inay ethay eet,stray ecausebay ehay athhay
akenedway ythay ogday atthay athhay ainlay asleepay inay ethay unsay. Idstday outhay otnay allfay
outay ithway aay ailortay orfay earingway ishay ewnay oubletday eforebay Easter?ay ithway
anotheray orfay yingtay ishay ewnay oesshay ithway anay olday iband?ray Anday yetay outhay iltway
utortay emay omfray uarrelling!qay

ENVOLIObay.
Anday Iay ereway osay aptay otay uarrelqay asay outhay art,ay anyay anmay ouldshay uybay ethay eefay
implesay ofay ymay ifelay orfay anay ourhay anday aay uarterqay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ethay eefay imple!say Oay imple!say

Enteray Ybalttay anday others.ay

ENVOLIObay.
Ybay ymay ead,hay erehay omescay ethay Apuletscay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Ybay ymay eel,hay Iay arecay otnay.

Entlemen,gay ood-den:gay aay ordway ithway oneay ofay you.ay

ordway anday aay owblay.

occasion.ay

ERCUTIOmay.
Ouldcay youay otnay aketay omesay occasionay ithoutway iving?gay

Ercutio,may outhay onsortestcay ithway Omeoray.

ERCUTIOmay.
Onsort?cay At,whay ostday outhay akemay usay instrels?may Anday outhay akemay instrelsmay ofay
us,ay ooklay otay earhay othingnay utbay iscordsday. Ere’shay ymay iddlestick,fay ere’shay
atthay allshay akemay youay anceday. Ounds,zay onsort!cay

ENVOLIObay.
Eway alktay erehay inay ethay ublicpay aunthay ofay enmay.
Eitheray ithdrawway untoay omesay ivatepray ace,play
Anday easonray oldlycay ofay youray ievances,gray
Oray elseay epart;day erehay allay eyesay azegay onay us.ay

ERCUTIOmay.
En’smay eyesay ereway ademay otay ook,lay anday etlay emthay azegay.
Iay illway otnay udgebay orfay onay an’smay easure,play I.ay

Enteray Omeoray.

YBALTtay.
Ell,way eacepay ebay ithway you,ay ir,say erehay omescay ymay anmay.

ERCUTIOmay.

Youray orshipway inay atthay ensesay aymay allcay imhay anmay.

YBALTtay.
Omeo,ray ethay ovelay Iay earbay eethay ancay afforday
Onay etterbay ermtay anthay is:thay Outhay artay aay illainvay.

OMEOray.

Othday uchmay excuseay ethay appertainingay ageray
Otay uchsay aay eetinggray. Illainvay amay Iay one;nay
Ereforethay arewell;fay Iay eesay outhay ow’stknay emay otnay.

YBALTtay.
Oy,bay isthay allshay otnay excuseay ethay injuriesay
Atthay outhay asthay oneday e,may ereforethay urntay anday awdray.

OMEOray.

Asay earlyday asay inemay own,ay ebay atisfiedsay.

ERCUTIOmay.
Oay alm,cay ishonourable,day ilevay ubmission!say
Aws._][_Dray Allaay occatastay arriescay itay away.ay

Awing._][_Dray Iay amay orfay you.ay

OMEOray.
Ourage,cay an;may ethay urthay annotcay ebay uchmay.

avegray anmay. Iay amay eppered,pay Iay arrant,way orfay isthay orldway. Aay agueplay o’ay othbay
youray ouseshay. Ounds,zay aay og,day aay at,ray aay ouse,may aay at,cay otay atchscray aay anmay otay

OMEOray.

Iay avehay it,ay anday oundlysay ootay. Youray ouses!hay

OMEOray.
Isthay entleman,gay ethay Ince’spray earnay ally,ay
Ymay eryvay iend,fray athhay otgay ishay ortalmay urthay

Athhay eenbay ymay ousincay. Oay eetsway Uliet,jay
Ythay eautybay athhay ademay emay effeminateay
Anday inay ymay empertay often’dsay alour’svay eelstay.

ENVOLIObay.

Atthay atelay outhay av’stgay e,may orfay Ercutio’smay oulsay

Ayingstay orfay inethay otay eepkay imhay ompanycay.

IRSTfay ITIZENcay.

INCEpRay.

ENVOLIObay.

Erethay ieslay ethay an,may ainslay ybay youngay Omeo,ray
Atthay ewslay ythay insman,kay avebray Ercutiomay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Ybalt,tay ymay ousin!cay Oay ymay other’sbray ild!chay
Oay Ince!pray Oay usband!hay O,ay ethay oodblay isay ill’dspay
Ofay ymay earday insman!kay Ince,pray asay outhay artay ue,tray
Orfay oodblay ofay oursay edshay oodblay ofay Ontaguemay.
Oay ousin,cay ousincay.

INCEpRay.
Envolio,bay owhay eganbay isthay oodyblay ay?fray

ENVOLIObay.
Ybalt,tay erehay ain,slay omwhay Omeo’sray andhay idday ay;slay
Omeo,ray atthay okespay imhay air,fay idbay imhay ethinkbay
Owhay icenay ethay uarrelqay as,way anday urg’day ithalway
Youray ighhay ispleasureday. Allay isthay uttereday
Ithway entlegay eath,bray almcay ook,lay eesknay umblyhay ow’dbay
Ouldcay otnay aketay ucetray ithway ethay unrulyay eensplay
Ofay Ybalt,tay eafday otay eace,pay utbay atthay ehay iltstay
Ithway iercingpay eelstay atay oldbay Ercutio’smay east,bray
O,whay allay asay ot,hay urnstay eadlyday ointpay otay oint,pay
And,ay ithway aay artialmay orn,scay ithway oneay andhay eatsbay
Oldcay eathday aside,ay anday ithway ethay otheray endssay
Itay ackbay otay Ybalt,tay osewhay exterityday
Etortsray it.ay Omeoray ehay iescray aloud,ay
Old,‘Hay iends!fray Iends,fray art!’pay anday iftersway anthay ishay ongue,tay
Ishay agileay armay eatsbay ownday eirthay atalfay oints,pay
Anday Ixt’tway emthay ushes;ray underneathay osewhay armay
Anay enviousay ustthray omfray Ybalttay ithay ethay ifelay
Ofay outstay Ercutio,may anday enthay Ybalttay edflay.
Utbay ybay anday ybay omescay ackbay otay Omeo,ray
Owhay adhay utbay ewlynay entertain’day evenge,ray
Anday o’ttay eythay ogay ikelay ightning;lay or,fay ereay Iay
Ouldcay awdray otay artpay emthay asway outstay Ybalttay ain;slay
Anday asay ehay ellfay idday Omeoray urntay anday yflay.
Isthay isay ethay uth,tray oray etlay Envoliobay ieday.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Ehay isay aay insmankay otay ethay Ontaguemay.
Affectionay akesmay imhay alse,fay ehay eaksspay otnay uetray.
Omesay entytway ofay emthay oughtfay inay isthay ackblay ife,stray
Anday allay osethay entytway ouldcay utbay illkay oneay ifelay.
Iay egbay orfay ustice,jay ichwhay ou,thay Ince,pray ustmay ive;gay
Omeoray ewslay Ybalt,tay Omeoray ustmay otnay ivelay.

INCEpRay.
Omeoray ewslay im,hay ehay ewslay Ercutiomay.
Owhay ownay ethay icepray ofay ishay earday oodblay othday owe?ay

ONTAGUEmay.
Otnay Omeo,ray Ince,pray ehay asway Ercutio’smay iend;fray
Ishay aultfay oncludescay utbay atwhay ethay awlay ouldshay end,ay
Ethay ifelay ofay Ybalttay.

INCEpRay.
Anday orfay atthay offenceay
Immediatelyay eway oday exileay imhay encehay.
Iay avehay anay interestay inay youray ate’shay oceeding,pray
Ymay oodblay orfay youray uderay awlsbray othday ielay a-bleeding.ay
Utbay I’llay amerceay youay ithway osay ongstray aay inefay
Atthay youay allshay allay epentray ethay osslay ofay inemay.
Iay illway ebay eafday otay eadingplay anday excuses;ay
Ornay earstay ornay ayerspray allshay urchasepay outay abuses.ay
Ereforethay useay onenay. Etlay Omeoray encehay inay aste,hay
Else,ay enwhay ehay isay ound,fay atthay ourhay isay ishay astlay.
Earbay encehay isthay ody,bay anday attenday ouray illway.
Ercymay utbay urders,may ardoningpay osethay atthay illkay.

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay II.ay Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

Enteray Ulietjay.

ULIETjay.
Allopgay apace,ay youay iery-footedfay eeds,stay
Owardstay Oebus’phay odginglay. Uchsay aay aggonerway
Asay Aetonphay ouldway ipwhay youay otay ethay estway
Anday ingbray inay oudyclay ightnay immediately.ay
Eadspray ythay oseclay urtain,cay ove-performinglay ight,nay
Atthay unaway’sray eyesay aymay ink,way anday Omeoray
Eaplay otay esethay arms,ay untalk’day ofay anday unseen.ay
Overslay ancay eesay otay oday eirthay amorousay itesray
Ybay eirthay ownay eauties:bay or,ay ifay ovelay ebay ind,blay
Itay estbay agreesay ithway ightnay. Ome,cay ivilcay ight,nay
Outhay ober-suitedsay atron,may allay inay ack,blay
Anday earnlay emay owhay otay oselay aay inningway atch,may
Ay’dplay orfay aay airpay ofay ainlessstay aidenhoodsmay.
Oodhay ymay unmann’day ood,blay atingbay inay ymay eeks,chay
Ithway ythay ackblay antle,may illtay angestray ove,lay owgray old,bay
Inkthay uetray ovelay acteday implesay odestymay.
Ome,cay ight,nay omecay Omeo;ray ome,cay outhay ayday inay ight;nay
Orfay outhay iltway ielay uponay ethay ingsway ofay ightnay
Iterwhay anthay ewnay owsnay uponay aay aven’sray ackbay.
Omecay entlegay ight,nay omecay ovinglay ack-brow’dblay ight,nay
Ivegay emay ymay Omeo,ray anday enwhay Iay allshay ie,day
Aketay imhay anday utcay imhay outay inay ittlelay ars,stay
Anday ehay illway akemay ethay acefay ofay eavenhay osay inefay
Atthay allay ethay orldway illway ebay inay ovelay ithway ight,nay
Anday aypay onay orshipway otay ethay arishgay unsay.
O,ay Iay avehay oughtbay ethay ansionmay ofay aay ove,lay
Utbay otnay ossess’dpay it;ay anday oughthay Iay amay old,say
Otnay yetay enjoy’d.ay Osay edioustay isay isthay ayday
Asay isay ethay ightnay eforebay omesay estivalfay
Otay anay impatientay ildchay atthay athhay ewnay obesray
Anday aymay otnay earway emthay. O,ay erehay omescay ymay Urse,nay
Anday eshay ingsbray ews,nay anday everyay onguetay atthay eaksspay
Utbay Omeo’sray amenay eaksspay eavenlyhay eloquence.ay

Enteray Urse,nay ithway ordscay.

Ow,nay Urse,nay atwhay ews?nay Atwhay asthay outhay ere?thay
Ethay ordscay atthay Omeoray idbay eethay etch?fay

URSEnay.
Ay,ay ay,ay ethay ordscay.

Ows[_Thray emthay own._]day

ULIETjay.
Ayay e,may atwhay ews?nay Ywhay ostday outhay ingwray ythay ands?hay

URSEnay.
Ah,ay ell-a-day,way e’shay ead,day e’shay ead,day e’shay ead!day
Eway areay undone,ay ady,lay eway areay undone.ay
Alackay ethay ay,day e’shay one,gay e’shay ill’d,kay e’shay eadday.

ULIETjay.
Ancay eavenhay ebay osay envious?ay

URSEnay.
Omeoray an,cay
Oughthay eavenhay annotcay. Oay Omeo,ray Omeoray.
Owhay everay ouldway avehay oughtthay it?ay Omeo!ray

ULIETjay.
Atwhay evilday artay ou,thay atthay ostday ormenttay emay us?thay
Isthay orturetay ouldshay ebay oar’dray inay ismalday ellhay.
Athhay Omeoray ainslay imself?hay Aysay outhay utbay Ay,ay
Anday atthay arebay owelvay Iay allshay oisonpay oremay
Anthay ethay eath-dartingday eyeay ofay ockatricecay.
Iay amay otnay Iay ifay erethay ebay uchsay anay I;ay
Oray osethay eyesay utshay atthay akemay eethay answeray Ay.ay
Ifay ehay ebay ain,slay aysay Ay;ay oray ifay ot,nay Onay.
Iefbray oundssay etermineday ofay ymay ealway oray oeway.

URSEnay.
Iay awsay ethay ound,way Iay awsay itay ithway inemay eyes,ay
Odgay avesay ethay ark!—heremay onay ishay anlymay eastbray.
Aay iteouspay orse,cay aay oodyblay iteouspay orse;cay
Ale,pay alepay asay ashes,ay allay edaub’dbay inay ood,blay
Allay inay ore-bloodgay. Iay oundedsway atay ethay ightsay.

ULIETjay.
O,ay eak,bray ymay earthay. Oorpay ankrout,bay eakbray atay once.ay
Otay ison,pray eyes;ay e’ernay ooklay onay ibertylay.
Ilevay earthay otay earthay esign;ray enday otionmay ere,hay
Anday outhay anday Omeoray esspray oneay eavyhay ierbay.

URSEnay.
Oay Ybalt,tay Ybalt,tay ethay estbay iendfray Iay adhay.
Oay ourteouscay Ybalt,tay onesthay entleman!gay
Atthay everay Iay ouldshay ivelay otay eesay eethay eadday.

ULIETjay.
Atwhay ormstay isay isthay atthay owsblay osay ontrary?cay
Isay Omeoray aughter’dslay anday isay Ybalttay ead?day
Ymay earestday ousin,cay anday ymay earerday ord?lay
Enthay eadfuldray umpettray oundsay ethay eneralgay oom,day
Orfay owhay isay iving,lay ifay osethay otway areay one?gay

URSEnay.
Ybalttay isay one,gay anday Omeoray anished,bay
Omeoray atthay ill’dkay im,hay ehay isay anishedbay.

ULIETjay.
Oay Od!gay Idday Omeo’sray andhay edshay Ybalt’stay ood?blay

URSEnay.
Itay id,day itay id;day alasay ethay ay,day itay idday.

ULIETjay.
Oay erpentsay eart,hay idhay ithway aay oweringflay ace!fay
Idday everay agondray eepkay osay airfay aay ave?cay
Eautifulbay yrant,tay iendfay angelical,ay
Ove-feather’dday aven,ray olvish-raveningway amb!lay
Espisedday ubstancesay ofay ivinestday ow!shay
Ustjay oppositeay otay atwhay outhay ustlyjay eem’st,say
Aay amnedday aint,say anay onourablehay illain!vay
Oay ature,nay atwhay adsthay outhay otay oday inay ellhay
Enwhay outhay idstday owerbay ethay iritspay ofay aay iendfay
Inay ortalmay aradisepay ofay uchsay eetsway esh?flay
Asway everay ookbay ontainingcay uchsay ilevay attermay
Osay airlyfay ound?bay O,ay atthay eceitday ouldshay elldway
Inay uchsay aay orgeousgay alacepay.

URSEnay.
Ere’sthay onay ust,tray
Onay aith,fay onay onestyhay inay enmay. Allay erjur’d,pay
Allay orsworn,fay allay aught,nay allay issemblersday.
Ah,ay ere’swhay ymay an?may Ivegay emay omesay aquaay itaevay.
Esethay iefs,gray esethay oes,way esethay orrowssay akemay emay old.ay
Ameshay omecay otay Omeoray.

ULIETjay.
Ister’dblay ebay ythay onguetay
Orfay uchsay aay ish!way Ehay asway otnay ornbay otay ameshay.
Uponay ishay owbray ameshay isay asham’day otay it;say
Orfay Is’tay aay onethray erewhay onourhay aymay ebay own’dcray
Olesay onarchmay ofay ethay universalay earth.ay
O,ay atwhay aay eastbay asway Iay otay idechay atay im!hay

URSEnay.
Illway youay eakspay ellway ofay imhay atthay ill’dkay youray ousin?cay

ULIETjay.
Allshay Iay eakspay illay ofay imhay atthay isay ymay usband?hay
Ah,ay oorpay ymay ord,lay atwhay onguetay allshay oothsmay ythay ame,nay
Enwhay Iay ythay ee-hours’thray ifeway avehay angledmay it?ay
Utbay erefore,whay illain,vay idstday outhay illkay ymay ousin?cay
Atthay illainvay ousincay ouldway avehay ill’dkay ymay usbandhay.
Ack,bay oolishfay ears,tay ackbay otay youray ativenay ing,spray
Youray ibutarytray opsdray elongbay otay oe,way
Ichwhay youay istakingmay offeray upay otay oyjay.
Ymay usbandhay ives,lay atthay Ybalttay ouldway avehay ain,slay
Anday Ybalt’stay ead,day atthay ouldway avehay ainslay ymay usbandhay.
Allay isthay isay omfort;cay ereforewhay eepway Iay en?thay
Omesay ordway erethay as,way orserway anthay Ybalt’stay eath,day
Atthay urder’dmay emay. Iay ouldway orgetfay itay ain,fay
Utbay O,ay itay essespray otay ymay emorymay
Ikelay amnedday uiltygay eedsday otay inners’say indsmay.
Ybalttay isay ead,day anday Omeoray anishedbay.
Atthay Anished,’‘bay atthay oneay ordway Anished,’‘bay
Athhay ainslay entay ousandthay Ybaltstay. Ybalt’stay eathday
Asway oeway enough,ay ifay itay adhay endeday erethay.
Oray ifay oursay oeway elightsday inay ellowship,fay
Anday eedlynay illway ebay ank’dray ithway otheray iefs,gray
Ywhay ollow’dfay ot,nay enwhay eshay aidsay Ybalt’stay ead,day
Ythay atherfay oray ythay other,may aynay oray oth,bay
Ichwhay odernmay amentationlay ightmay avehay ov’d?may
Utbay ithway aay ear-wardray ollowingfay Ybalt’stay eath,day
Omeo‘Ray isay anished’—tobay eakspay atthay ordway
Isay ather,fay other,may Ybalt,tay Omeo,ray Uliet,jay
Allay ain,slay allay eadday. Omeoray isay anished,bay
Erethay isay onay end,ay onay imit,lay easure,may ound,bay
Inay atthay ord’sway eath,day onay ordsway ancay atthay oeway oundsay.
Erewhay isay ymay atherfay anday ymay other,may Urse?nay

URSEnay.
Eepingway anday ailingway overay Ybalt’stay orsecay.
Illway youay ogay otay em?thay Iay illway ingbray youay itherthay.

ULIETjay.
Ashway eythay ishay oundsway ithway earstay. Inemay allshay ebay ent,spay
Enwhay eirsthay areay y,dray orfay Omeo’sray anishmentbay.
Aketay upay osethay ordscay. Oorpay opes,ray youay areay eguil’d,bay
Othbay youay anday I;ay orfay Omeoray isay exil’d.ay
Ehay ademay youay orfay aay ighwayhay otay ymay ed,bay
Utbay I,ay aay aid,may ieday aiden-widowedmay.
Omecay ords,cay omecay Urse,nay I’llay otay ymay eddingway ed,bay
Anday eath,day otnay Omeo,ray aketay ymay aidenheadmay.

URSEnay.
Iehay otay youray amberchay. I’llay indfay Omeoray
Otay omfortcay you.ay Iay otway ellway erewhay ehay is.ay
Arkhay ye,ay youray Omeoray illway ebay erehay atay ightnay.
I’llay otay im,hay ehay isay idhay atay Awrence’lay ellcay.

ULIETjay.
Oay indfay im,hay ivegay isthay ingray otay ymay uetray ight,knay
Anday idbay imhay omecay otay aketay ishay astlay arewellfay.

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay III.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay ellcay.

Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Omeo,ray omecay orth;fay omecay orth,fay outhay earfulfay anmay.
Afflictionay isay enanmour’day ofay ythay artspay
Anday outhay artay eddedway otay alamitycay.

Enteray Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Ather,fay atwhay ews?nay Atwhay isay ethay Ince’spray oom?day
Atwhay orrowsay avescray acquaintanceay atay ymay and,hay
Atthay Iay yetay owknay ot?nay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Ootay amiliarfay
Isay ymay earday onsay ithway uchsay oursay ompanycay.
Iay ingbray eethay idingstay ofay ethay Ince’spray oomday.

OMEOray.
Atwhay esslay anthay oomsdayday isay ethay Ince’spray oom?day

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Aay entlergay udgmentjay anish’dvay omfray ishay ips,lay
Otnay ody’sbay eath,day utbay ody’sbay anishmentbay.

OMEOray.
A,hay anishment?bay Ebay erciful,may aysay eath;day
Orfay exileay athhay oremay errortay inay ishay ook,lay
Uchmay oremay anthay eathday. Oday otnay aysay anishmentbay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Encehay omfray Eronavay artay outhay anishedbay.
Ebay atient,pay orfay ethay orldway isay oadbray anday ideway.

OMEOray.
Erethay isay onay orldway ithoutway Eronavay alls,way
Utbay urgatory,pay orture,tay ellhay itself.ay
Encehay anishedbay isay anish’dbay omfray ethay orld,way
Anday orld’sway exileay isay eathday. Enthay anishedbay
Isay eathday isterm’dmay. Allingcay eathday anished,bay
Outhay utt’stcay ymay eadhay offay ithway aay oldengay axe,ay
Anday ilestsmay uponay ethay okestray atthay urdersmay emay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Oay eadlyday in,say Oay uderay unthankfulness!ay
Ythay aultfay ouray awlay allscay eath,day utbay ethay indkay Ince,pray
Akingtay ythay art,pay athhay ush’dbray asideay ethay aw,lay
Anday urn’dtay atthay ackblay ordway eathday otay anishmentbay.
Isthay isay earday ercy,may anday outhay ee’stsay itay otnay.

OMEOray.
Is’Tay orture,tay anday otnay ercymay. Eavenhay isay erehay
Erewhay Ulietjay ives,lay anday everyay atcay anday og,day
Anday ittlelay ouse,may everyay unworthyay ing,thay
Ivelay erehay inay eavenhay anday aymay ooklay onay er,hay
Utbay Omeoray aymay otnay. Oremay alidity,vay
Oremay onourablehay ate,stay oremay ourtshipcay iveslay
Inay arrioncay iesflay anthay Omeoray. Eythay aymay eizesay
Onay ethay itewhay onderway ofay earday Uliet’sjay and,hay
Anday ealstay immortalay essingblay omfray erhay ips,lay
O,whay evenay inay urepay anday estalvay odestymay
Illstay ush,blay asay inkingthay eirthay ownay isseskay insay.
Utbay Omeoray aymay ot,nay ehay isay anishedbay.
Isthay aymay iesflay o,day enwhay Iay omfray isthay ustmay yflay.
Eythay areay eefray enmay utbay Iay amay anishedbay.
Anday ay’stsay outhay yetay atthay exileay isay otnay eath?day
Adsthay outhay onay oisonpay ix’d,may onay arp-groundshay ife,knay
Onay uddensay eanmay ofay eath,day oughthay e’ernay osay ean,may
Utbay anishedbay otay illkay e?may Anished?bay
Oay Iar,fray ethay amnedday useay atthay ordway inay ellhay.
Owlinghay attendsay it.ay Owhay asthay outhay ethay eart,hay
Eingbay aay ivine,day aay ostlyghay onfessor,cay
Aay in-absolver,say anday ymay iendfray ofess’d,pray
Otay anglemay emay ithway atthay ordway anished?bay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Outhay ondfay admay an,may earhay emay eakspay aay ittle,lay

OMEOray.
O,ay outhay iltway eakspay againay ofay anishmentbay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
I’llay ivegay eethay armouray otay eepkay offay atthay ord,way
Adversity’say eetsway ilk,may ilosophy,phay
Otay omfortcay ee,thay oughthay outhay artay anishedbay.

OMEOray.
Yetay anished?bay Anghay upay ilosophyphay.
Unlessay ilosophyphay ancay akemay aay Uliet,jay
Isplantday aay own,tay everseray aay Ince’spray oom,day
Itay elpshay ot,nay itay evailspray ot,nay alktay onay oremay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
O,ay enthay Iay eesay atthay admay enmay avehay onay ears.ay

OMEOray.
Owhay ouldshay ey,thay enwhay atthay iseway enmay avehay onay eyes?ay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Etlay emay isputeday ithway eethay ofay ythay estate.ay

OMEOray.
Outhay anstcay otnay eakspay ofay atthay outhay ostday otnay eelfay.
Ertway outhay asay youngay asay I,ay Ulietjay ythay ove,lay
Anay ourhay utbay arried,may Ybalttay urdered,may
Otingday ikelay e,may anday ikelay emay anished,bay
Enthay ightstmay outhay eak,spay enthay ightstmay outhay eartay ythay air,hay
Anday allfay uponay ethay oundgray asay Iay oday ow,nay
Akingtay ethay easuremay ofay anay unmadeay avegray.

Ocking[_Knay ithin._]way

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Arise;ay oneay ocksknay. Oodgay Omeo,ray idehay yselfthay.

OMEOray.
Otnay I,ay unlessay ethay eathbray ofay eartsickhay oansgray
Ist-likemay infolday emay omfray ethay earchsay ofay eyes.ay

Ocking._][_Knay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Ark,hay owhay eythay ock!—Who’sknay ere?—Romeo,thay arise,ay
Outhay iltway ebay aken.—Staytay awhile.—Standay up.ay

Ocking._][_Knay

Unray otay ymay udy.—By-and-by.—God’sstay ill,way
Atwhay implenesssay isay is.—Ithay ome,cay Iay omecay.

Ocking._][_Knay

Owhay ocksknay osay ard?hay Encewhay omecay you,ay at’swhay youray ill?way

URSEnay.
Ithin._][_Way Etlay emay omecay in,ay anday youay allshay owknay ymay errand.ay
Iay omecay omfray Adylay Ulietjay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Elcomeway enthay.

Enteray Ursenay.

URSEnay.
Oay olyhay Iar,fray O,ay elltay e,may olyhay Iar,fray
Erewhay isay ymay ady’slay ord,lay ere’swhay Omeo?ray

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Erethay onay ethay ound,gray ithway ishay ownay earstay ademay unkdray.

URSEnay.
O,ay ehay isay evenay inay ymay istress’may asecay.
Ustjay inay erhay ase!cay Oay oefulway ympathy!say
Iteouspay edicamentpray. Evenay osay ieslay e,shay
Ubberingblay anday eeping,way eepingway anday ubberingblay.
Andstay up,ay andstay up;ay and,stay anday youay ebay aay anmay.
Orfay Uliet’sjay ake,say orfay erhay ake,say iseray anday andstay.
Ywhay ouldshay youay allfay intoay osay eepday anay O?ay

OMEOray.
Ursenay.

URSEnay.
Ahay ir,say ahay ir,say eath’sday ethay enday ofay all.ay

OMEOray.
Akestspay outhay ofay Uliet?jay Owhay isay itay ithway er?hay
Othday otnay eshay inkthay emay anay olday urderer,may
Ownay Iay avehay ain’dstay ethay ildhoodchay ofay ouray oyjay
Ithway oodblay emov’dray utbay ittlelay omfray erhay own?ay
Erewhay isay e?shay Anday owhay othday e?shay Anday atwhay ayssay
Ymay onceal’dcay adylay otay ouray ancell’dcay ove?lay

URSEnay.
O,ay eshay ayssay othing,nay ir,say utbay eepsway anday eeps;way
Anday ownay allsfay onay erhay ed,bay anday enthay artsstay up,ay
Anday Ybalttay alls,cay anday enthay onay Omeoray ies,cray
Anday enthay ownday allsfay again.ay

OMEOray.
Asay ifay atthay ame,nay
Otshay omfray ethay eadlyday evellay ofay aay un,gay
Idday urdermay er,hay asay atthay ame’snay ursedcay andhay
Urder’dmay erhay insmankay. O,ay elltay e,may Iar,fray elltay e,may
Inay atwhay ilevay artpay ofay isthay anatomyay
Othday ymay amenay odge?lay Elltay e,may atthay Iay aymay acksay
Ethay atefulhay ansionmay.

Awing[_Dray ishay ord._]sway

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Oldhay ythay esperateday andhay.
Artay outhay aay an?may Ythay ormfay iescray outay outhay art.ay
Ythay earstay areay omanish,way ythay ildway actsay enoteday
Ethay unreasonableay uryfay ofay aay eastbay.
Unseemlyay omanway inay aay eemingsay an,may
Anday ill-beseemingay eastbay inay eemingsay oth!bay
Outhay asthay amaz’day emay. Ybay ymay olyhay order,ay
Iay oughtthay ythay ispositionday etterbay emper’dtay.
Asthay outhay ainslay Ybalt?tay Iltway outhay ayslay yself?thay
Anday ayslay ythay ady,lay atthay inay ythay ifelay ives,lay
Ybay oingday amnedday atehay uponay yself?thay
Ywhay ail’stray outhay onay ythay irth,bay ethay eavenhay anday earth?ay
Incesay irth,bay anday eavenhay anday earth,ay allay eethray oday eetmay
Inay eethay atay once;ay ichwhay outhay atay onceay ouldstway oselay.
Ie,fay ie,fay outhay am’stshay ythay ape,shay ythay ove,lay ythay it,way
Ich,whay ikelay aay usurer,ay abound’stay inay all,ay
Anday usestay onenay inay atthay uetray useay indeeday
Ichwhay ouldshay edeckbay ythay ape,shay ythay ove,lay ythay itway.
Ythay oblenay apeshay isay utbay aay ormfay ofay ax,way
Igressingday omfray ethay alourvay ofay aay an;may
Ythay earday ovelay ornsway utbay ollowhay erjury,pay
Illingkay atthay ovelay ichwhay outhay asthay ow’dvay otay erish;chay
Ythay it,way atthay ornamentay otay apeshay anday ove,lay
Isshapenmay inay ethay onductcay ofay emthay oth,bay
Ikelay owderpay inay aay illessskay oldier’ssay ask,flay
Isay etsay afireay ybay inethay ownay ignorance,ay
Anday outhay ismember’dday ithway inethay ownay efenceday.
At,whay ouseray ee,thay anmay. Ythay Ulietjay isay alive,ay
Orfay osewhay earday akesay outhay astway utbay atelylay eadday.
Erethay artay outhay appyhay. Ybalttay ouldway illkay ee,thay
Utbay outhay ew’stslay Ybalt;tay erethay artay outhay appyhay.
Ethay awlay atthay eaten’dthray eathday ecomesbay ythay iend,fray
Anday urnstay itay otay exile;ay erethay artay outhay appyhay.
Aay ackpay ofay essingsblay ightlay uponay ythay ack;bay
Appinesshay ourtscay eethay inay erhay estbay array;ay
Utbay ikelay aay isshapedmay anday ullensay ench,way
Outhay utt’stpay upay ythay Ortunefay anday ythay ovelay.
Aketay eed,hay aketay eed,hay orfay uchsay ieday iserablemay.
O,gay etgay eethay otay ythay ovelay asay asway ecreed,day
Ascenday erhay amber,chay encehay anday omfortcay erhay.
Utbay ooklay outhay aystay otnay illtay ethay atchway ebay et,say
Orfay enthay outhay anstcay otnay asspay otay Antua;may
Erewhay outhay altshay ivelay illtay eway ancay indfay aay imetay
Otay azeblay youray arriage,may econcileray youray iends,fray
Egbay ardonpay ofay ethay Ince,pray anday allcay eethay ackbay
Ithway entytway undredhay ousandthay imestay oremay oyjay
Anthay outhay ent’stway orthfay inay amentationlay.
Ogay efore,bay Ursenay. Ommendcay emay otay ythay ady,lay
Anday idbay erhay astenhay allay ethay ousehay otay ed,bay
Ichwhay eavyhay orrowsay akesmay emthay aptay unto.ay
Omeoray isay omingcay.

URSEnay.
Oay Ord,lay Iay ouldcay avehay ay’dstay erehay allay ethay ightnay
Otay earhay oodgay ounselcay. O,ay atwhay earninglay is!ay
Ymay ord,lay I’llay elltay ymay adylay youay illway omecay.

OMEOray.
Oday o,say anday idbay ymay eetsway eparepray otay idechay.

URSEnay.
Erehay ir,say aay ingray eshay idbay emay ivegay you,ay irsay.
Iehay you,ay akemay aste,hay orfay itay owsgray eryvay atelay.

Exit._][_ay

OMEOray.
Owhay ellway ymay omfortcay isay eviv’dray ybay isthay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Ogay ence,hay oodgay ight,nay anday erehay andsstay allay youray ate:stay
Eitheray ebay onegay eforebay ethay atchway ebay et,say
Oray ybay ethay eakbray ofay ayday isguis’dday omfray encehay.
Ojournsay inay Antuamay. I’llay indfay outay youray an,may
Anday ehay allshay ignifysay omfray imetay otay imetay
Everyay oodgay aphay otay youay atthay anceschay erehay.
Ivegay emay ythay and;hay Is’tay ate;lay arewell;fay oodgay ightnay.

OMEOray.
Utbay atthay aay oyjay astpay oyjay allscay outay onay e,may
Itay ereway aay iefgray osay iefbray otay artpay ithway eethay.
Arewellfay.

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay IV.ay Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

Enteray Apulet,cay Adylay Apuletcay anday Arispay.

APULETcay.
Ingsthay avehay allenfay out,ay ir,say osay unluckilyay
Atthay eway avehay adhay onay imetay otay ovemay ouray aughterday.
Ooklay you,ay eshay ov’dlay erhay insmankay Ybalttay early,day
Anday osay idday I.ay Ell,way eway ereway ornbay otay ieday.
Is’Tay eryvay ate;lay e’llshay otnay omecay ownday onighttay.
Iay omisepray you,ay utbay orfay youray ompany,cay
Iay ouldway avehay eenbay abeday anay ourhay ago.ay

ARISpay.
Esethay imestay ofay oeway afforday onay unetay otay ooway.
Adam,may oodgay ightnay. Ommendcay emay otay youray aughterday.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Iay ill,way anday owknay erhay indmay earlyay omorrow;tay
Onighttay e’sshay ew’dmay upay otay erhay eavinesshay.

APULETcay.
Irsay Aris,pay Iay illway akemay aay esperateday endertay
Ofay ymay ild’schay ovelay. Iay inkthay eshay illway ebay ul’dray
Inay allay espectsray ybay e;may aynay ore,may Iay oubtday itay otnay.
Ife,way ogay youay otay erhay ereay youay ogay otay ed,bay
Acquaintay erhay erehay ofay ymay onsay Aris’pay ove,lay
Anday idbay er,hay arkmay youay e,may onay Ednesdayway ext,nay
Ut,bay oft,say atwhay ayday isay is?thay

ARISpay.
Onday,may ymay ordlay.

APULETcay.
Onday!may A,hay a!hay Ell,way Ednesdayway isay ootay oon,say
Aay Ursdaythay etlay itay e;bay aay Ursday,thay elltay er,hay
Eshay allshay ebay arriedmay otay isthay oblenay earl.ay
Illway youay ebay eady?ray Oday youay ikelay isthay aste?hay
E’llway eepkay onay eatgray ado,—aay iendfray oray o,tway
Or,fay arkhay you,ay Ybalttay eingbay ainslay osay ate,lay
Itay aymay ebay oughtthay eway eldhay imhay arelessly,cay
Eingbay ouray insman,kay ifay eway evelray uchmay.
Ereforethay e’llway avehay omesay alfhay aay ozenday iends,fray
Anday erethay anay end.ay Utbay atwhay aysay youay otay Ursday?thay

ARISpay.
Ymay ord,lay Iay ouldway atthay Ursdaythay ereway omorrowtay.

APULETcay.
Ell,way etgay youay onegay. Aay Ursdaythay ebay itay enthay.
Ogay youay otay Ulietjay ereay youay ogay otay ed,bay
Eparepray er,hay ife,way againstay isthay eddingway ayday.
Arewell,fay ymay ord.—Lightlay otay ymay amber,chay o!hay
Aforeay e,may itay isay osay eryvay eryvay atelay atthay eway
Aymay allcay itay earlyay ybay anday ybay. Oodgay ightnay.

Exeunt._][_ay

ENEsCay vay. Anay openay Allerygay otay Uliet’sjay Amber,chay overlookingay ethay Ardengay.

Enteray Omeoray anday Ulietjay.

ULIETjay.
Iltway outhay ebay one?gay Itay isay otnay yetay earnay ayday.
Itay asway ethay ightingale,nay anday otnay ethay ark,lay
Atthay ierc’dpay ethay earfulfay ollowhay ofay inethay ear;ay
Ightlynay eshay ingssay onay yonday omegranatepay eetray.
Elievebay e,may ove,lay itay asway ethay ightingalenay.

OMEOray.
Itay asway ethay ark,lay ethay eraldhay ofay ethay orn,may
Onay ightingalenay. Ook,lay ove,lay atwhay enviousay eaksstray
Oday acelay ethay everingsay oudsclay inay yonderay east.ay
Ight’snay andlescay areay urntbay out,ay anday ocundjay ayday
Andsstay iptoetay onay ethay istymay ountainmay opstay.
Iay ustmay ebay onegay anday ive,lay oray aystay anday ieday.

ULIETjay.
Yonday ightlay isay otnay aylight,day Iay owknay it,ay I.ay
Itay isay omesay eteormay atthay ethay unsay exhalesay
Otay ebay otay eethay isthay ightnay aay orchbearertay
Anday ightlay eethay onay ythay ayway otay Antuamay.
Ereforethay aystay yet,ay outhay eed’stnay otnay otay ebay onegay.

OMEOray.
Etlay emay ebay a’en,tay etlay emay ebay utpay otay eath,day
Iay amay ontent,cay osay outhay iltway avehay itay osay.
I’llay aysay yonay eygray isay otnay ethay orning’smay eye,ay
Is’Tay utbay ethay alepay eflexray ofay Ynthia’scay owbray.
Ornay atthay isay otnay ethay arklay osewhay otesnay oday eatbay
Ethay aultyvay eavenhay osay ighhay aboveay ouray eadshay.
Iay avehay oremay arecay otay aystay anthay illway otay ogay.
Ome,cay eath,day anday elcomeway. Ulietjay illsway itay osay.
Owhay is’t,ay ymay oul?say Et’slay alktay. Itay isay otnay ayday.

ULIETjay.
Itay is,ay itay is!ay Iehay ence,hay ebay one,gay away.ay
Itay isay ethay arklay atthay ingssay osay outay ofay une,tay
Ainingstray arshhay iscordsday anday unpleasingay arpsshay.
Omesay aysay ethay arklay akesmay eetsway ivision;day
Isthay othday otnay o,say orfay eshay ividethday us.ay
Omesay aysay ethay arklay anday oathedlay oadtay angechay eyes.ay
O,ay ownay Iay ouldway eythay adhay ang’dchay oicesvay oo,tay
Incesay armay omfray armay atthay oicevay othday usay affray,ay
Untinghay eethay encehay ithway unt’s-uphay otay ethay ayday.
Oay ownay ebay one,gay oremay ightlay anday ightlay itay owsgray.

OMEOray.
Oremay ightlay anday ight,lay oremay arkday anday arkday ouray oesway.

ACTay IVay

ENEsCay I.ay Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.


Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay anday Arispay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Onay Ursday,thay ir?say Ethay imetay isay eryvay ortshay.

ARISpay.
Ymay atherfay Apuletcay illway avehay itay o;say
Anday Iay amay othingnay owslay otay ackslay ishay astehay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Youay aysay youay oday otnay owknay ethay ady’slay indmay.
Unevenay isay ethay ourse;cay Iay ikelay itay otnay.

ARISpay.
Immoderatelyay eshay eepsway orfay Ybalt’stay eath,day
Anday ereforethay avehay Iay ittlelay alk’dtay ofay ove;lay
Orfay Enusvay ilessmay otnay inay aay ousehay ofay earstay.
Ow,nay ir,say erhay atherfay ountscay itay angerousday
Atthay eshay oday ivegay erhay orrowsay osay uchmay ay;sway
Anday inay ishay isdom,way asteshay ouray arriage,may
Otay opstay ethay inundationay ofay erhay ears,tay
Ich,whay ootay uchmay indedmay ybay erselfhay alone,ay
Aymay ebay utpay omfray erhay ybay ocietysay.
Ownay oday youay owknay ethay easonray ofay isthay astehay.

Aside._][_ay Iay ouldway Iay ewknay otnay ywhay itay ouldshay ebay ow’d.—slay
