Odgay ieldshay Iay ouldshay isturbday evotion!—day
Uliet,jay onay Ursdaythay earlyay illway Iay ouseray ye,ay
Illtay en,thay adieu;ay anday eepkay isthay olyhay isskay.

Exit._][_ay

ULIETjay.
Oay utshay ethay oor,day anday enwhay outhay asthay oneday o,say
Omecay eepway ithway e,may astpay ope,hay astpay ure,cay astpay elp!hay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Oay Uliet,jay Iay alreadyay owknay ythay ief;gray
Itay ainsstray emay astpay ethay ompasscay ofay ymay itsway.
Iay earhay outhay ust,may anday othingnay aymay oroguepray it,ay
Onay Ursdaythay extnay ebay arriedmay otay isthay Ountycay.

ULIETjay.
Elltay emay ot,nay Iar,fray atthay outhay ear’sthay ofay is,thay
Unlessay outhay elltay emay owhay Iay aymay eventpray it.ay
Ifay inay ythay isdom,way outhay anstcay ivegay onay elp,hay
Oday outhay utbay allcay ymay esolutionray ise,way
Anday ithway isthay ifeknay I’llay elphay itay esentlypray.
Odgay oin’djay ymay earthay anday Omeo’s,ray outhay ouray ands;hay
Anday ereay isthay and,hay ybay eethay otay Omeo’sray eal’d,say
Allshay ebay ethay abellay otay anotheray eed,day
Oray ymay uetray earthay ithway eacheroustray evoltray
Urntay otay another,ay isthay allshay ayslay emthay othbay.
Erefore,thay outay ofay ythay ong-experienc’dlay ime,tay
Ivegay emay omesay esentpray ounsel,cay oray eholdbay
Ixt’Tway ymay extremesay anday emay isthay oodyblay ifeknay
Allshay ayplay ethay empire,ay arbitratingay atthay
Ichwhay ethay ommissioncay ofay ythay yearsay anday artay
Ouldcay otay onay issueay ofay uetray onourhay ingbray.
Ebay otnay osay onglay otay eakspay. Iay onglay otay ie,day
Ifay atwhay outhay eak’stspay eakspay otnay ofay emedyray.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Old,hay aughterday. Iay oday yspay aay indkay ofay ope,hay
Ichwhay avescray asay esperateday anay executionay
Asay atthay isay esperateday ichwhay eway ouldway eventpray.
If,ay atherray anthay otay arrymay Ountycay Arispay
Outhay asthay ethay engthstray ofay illway otay ayslay yself,thay
Enthay isay itay ikelylay outhay iltway undertakeay
Aay ingthay ikelay eathday otay idechay awayay isthay ame,shay
Atthay op’stcay ithway eathday imselfhay otay apescay omfray it.ay
Anday ifay outhay ar’st,day I’llay ivegay eethay emedyray.

ULIETjay.
O,ay idbay emay eap,lay atherray anthay arrymay Aris,pay
Omfray offay ethay attlementsbay ofay yonderay ower,tay
Oray alkway inay ievishthay ays,way oray idbay emay urklay
Erewhay erpentssay are.ay Ainchay emay ithway oaringray ears;bay
Oray idehay emay ightlynay inay aay arnel-house,chay
O’er-cover’day uiteqay ithway eadday en’smay attlingray ones,bay
Ithway eekyray anksshay anday yelloway aplesschay ullsskay.
Oray idbay emay ogay intoay aay ew-madenay ave,gray
Anday idehay emay ithway aay eadday anmay inay ishay oud;shray
Ingsthay at,thay otay earhay emthay old,tay avehay ademay emay emble,tray
Anday Iay illway oday itay ithoutway earfay oray oubt,day
Otay ivelay anay unstain’day ifeway otay ymay eetsway ovelay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Oldhay enthay. Ogay ome,hay ebay erry,may ivegay onsentcay
Otay arrymay Arispay. Ednesdayway isay omorrow;tay
Omorrowtay ightnay ooklay atthay outhay ielay alone,ay
Etlay otnay ythay Ursenay ielay ithway eethay inay ythay amberchay.
Aketay outhay isthay ial,vay eingbay enthay inay ed,bay
Anday isthay istilledday iquorlay inkdray outhay off,ay
Enwhay esentlypray oughthray allay ythay einsvay allshay unray
Aay oldcay anday owsydray umour;hay orfay onay ulsepay
Allshay eepkay ishay ativenay ogress,pray utbay urceasesay.
Onay armth,way onay eathbray allshay estifytay outhay ivest,lay
Ethay osesray inay ythay ipslay anday eekschay allshay adefay
Otay alypay ashes;ay ythay eyes’ay indowsway all,fay
Ikelay eathday enwhay ehay utsshay upay ethay ayday ofay ifelay.
Eachay artpay epriv’dday ofay upplesay overnment,gay
Allshay iffstay anday arkstay anday oldcay appearay ikelay eathday.
Anday inay isthay orrow’dbay ikenesslay ofay unkshray eathday
Outhay altshay ontinuecay otway anday ortyfay ours,hay
Anday enthay awakeay asay omfray aay easantplay eepslay.
Ownay enwhay ethay idegroombray inay ethay orningmay omescay
Otay ouseray eethay omfray ythay ed,bay erethay artay outhay eadday.
Enthay asay ethay annermay ofay ouray ountrycay is,ay
Inay ythay estbay obes,ray uncover’d,ay onay ethay ier,bay
Outhay altshay ebay ornebay otay atthay amesay ancientay aultvay
Erewhay allay ethay indredkay ofay ethay Apuletscay ielay.
Inay ethay eantime,may againstay outhay altshay awake,ay
Allshay Omeoray ybay ymay etterslay owknay ouray ift,dray
Anday itherhay allshay ehay ome,cay anday ehay anday Iay
Illway atchway ythay aking,way anday atthay eryvay ightnay
Allshay Omeoray earbay eethay encehay otay Antuamay.
Anday isthay allshay eefray eethay omfray isthay esentpray ame,shay
Ifay onay inconstantay oytay ornay omanishway earfay
Abateay ythay alourvay inay ethay actingay it.ay

ULIETjay.
Ivegay e,may ivegay e!may Oay elltay otnay emay ofay ear!fay

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Old;hay etgay youay one,gay ebay ongstray anday osperouspray
Inay isthay esolveray. I’llay endsay aay iarfray ithway eedspay
Otay Antua,may ithway ymay etterslay otay ythay ordlay.

ULIETjay.
Ovelay ivegay emay ength,stray anday engthstray allshay elphay afford.ay
Arewell,fay earday atherfay.

Exeunt._][_ay

ingersfay.

Eway allshay ebay uchmay unfurnish’day orfay isthay imetay.

URSEnay.
Ay,ay orsoothfay.

URSEnay.

APULETcay.

ULIETjay.
Erewhay Iay avehay earntlay emay otay epentray ethay insay
Ofay isobedientday oppositionay
Otay youay anday youray ehests;bay anday amay enjoin’day
Ybay olyhay Awrencelay otay allfay ostratepray ere,hay
Otay egbay youray ardonpay. Ardon,pay Iay eseechbay you.ay
Enceforwardhay Iay amay everay ul’dray ybay you.ay

APULETcay.
Endsay orfay ethay Ounty,cay ogay elltay imhay ofay isthay.

ULIETjay.
Iay etmay ethay youthfulay ordlay atay Awrence’lay ell,cay

APULETcay.
Y,whay Iay amay adglay on’t.ay Isthay isay ellway. Andstay up.ay

ULIETjay.

ADYlay APULETcay.

APULETcay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
Eway allshay ebay ortshay inay ouray ovision,pray
Is’Tay ownay earnay ightnay.

APULETcay.
Ush,tay Iay illway irstay about,ay
Anday allay ingsthay allshay ebay ell,way Iay arrantway ee,thay ifeway.
Ogay outhay otay Uliet,jay elphay otay eckday upay erhay.
I’llay otnay otay edbay onight,tay etlay emay alone.ay
I’llay ayplay ethay ousewifehay orfay isthay once.—What,ay o!—hay
Eythay areay allay orth:fay ell,way Iay illway alkway yselfmay
Otay Ountycay Aris,pay otay eparepray imhay upay
Againstay omorrowtay. Ymay earthay isay ondrousway ightlay

ENEsCay III.ay Uliet’sjay Amberchay.

Enteray Ulietjay anday Ursenay.

ULIETjay.
Ay,ay osethay attiresay areay estbay. Ut,bay entlegay Urse,nay
Iay aypray eethay eavelay emay otay yselfmay onight;tay
Orfay Iay avehay eednay ofay anymay orisonsay
Otay ovemay ethay eavenshay otay ilesmay uponay ymay ate,stay
Ich,whay ellway outhay ow’st,knay isay osscray anday ullfay ofay insay.

ADYlay APULETcay.
At,whay areay youay usy,bay o?hay Eednay youay ymay elp?hay

ULIETjay.

Asay areay ehovefulbay orfay ouray atestay omorrowtay.

Etgay eethay otay edbay anday est,ray orfay outhay asthay eednay.

ULIETjay.
Arewellfay. Odgay owsknay enwhay eway allshay eetmay again.ay
Iay avehay aay aintfay oldcay earfay illsthray oughthray ymay einsvay
Atthay almostay eezesfray upay ethay eathay ofay ifelay.
I’llay allcay emthay ackbay againay otay omfortcay emay.
Urse!—Whatnay ouldshay eshay oday ere?hay
Ymay ismalday enescay Iay eedsnay ustmay actay alone.ay
Ome,cay ialvay.
Atwhay ifay isthay ixturemay oday otnay orkway atay all?ay
Allshay Iay ebay arriedmay enthay omorrowtay orning?may
O,nay O!nay Isthay allshay orbidfay it.ay Ielay outhay erethay.

Aying[_Lay ownday erhay agger._]day

Atwhay ifay itay ebay aay oison,pay ichwhay ethay Iarfray
Ubtlysay athhay inister’dmay otay avehay emay ead,day
Estlay inay isthay arriagemay ehay ouldshay ebay ishonour’d,day
Ecausebay ehay arriedmay emay eforebay otay Omeo?ray
Iay earfay itay is.ay Anday yetay ethinksmay itay ouldshay ot,nay
Orfay ehay athhay illstay eenbay iedtray aay olyhay anmay.
Owhay if,ay enwhay Iay amay aidlay intoay ethay omb,tay
Iay akeway eforebay ethay imetay atthay Omeoray
Omecay otay edeemray e?may Ere’sthay aay earfulfay oint!pay
Allshay Iay otnay enthay ebay ifledstay inay ethay ault,vay
Otay osewhay oulfay outhmay onay ealthsomehay airay eathesbray in,ay
Anday erethay ieday angledstray ereay ymay Omeoray omes?cay
Or,ay ifay Iay ive,lay isay itay otnay eryvay ike,lay
Ethay orriblehay onceitcay ofay eathday anday ight,nay
Ogethertay ithway ethay errortay ofay ethay ace,play
Asay inay aay ault,vay anay ancientay eceptacle,ray
Erewhay orfay isthay anymay undredhay yearsay ethay onesbay
Ofay allay ymay uriedbay ancestorsay areay ack’d,pay
Erewhay oodyblay Ybalt,tay yetay utbay eengray inay earth,ay
Ieslay esteringfay inay ishay oud;shray ere,whay asay eythay ay,say
Atay omesay ourshay inay ethay ightnay iritsspay esort—ray
Alack,ay alack,ay isay itay otnay ikelay atthay I,ay
Osay earlyay aking,way atwhay ithway oathsomelay ells,smay
Anday ieksshray ikelay andrakesmay orntay outay ofay ethay earth,ay
Atthay ivinglay ortals,may earinghay em,thay unray admay.
O,ay ifay Iay ake,way allshay Iay otnay ebay istraught,day
Environeday ithway allay esethay ideoushay ears,fay
Anday adlymay ayplay ithway ymay orefathers’fay oints?jay
Anday uckplay ethay angledmay Ybalttay omfray ishay oud?shray
And,ay inay isthay age,ray ithway omesay eatgray insman’skay one,bay
Asay ithway aay ub,clay ashday outay ymay esperateday ains?bray
Oay ook,lay ethinksmay Iay eesay ymay ousin’scay ostghay
Eekingsay outay Omeoray atthay idday itspay ishay odybay
Uponay aay apier’sray ointpay. Ay,stay Ybalt,tay ay!stay
Omeo,ray Omeo,ray Omeo,ray ere’shay ink!dray Iay inkdray otay eethay.

Ows[_Thray erselfhay onay ethay ed._]bay

ENEsCay vay. Uliet’sjay Amber;chay Ulietjay onay ethay edbay.

Enteray Ursenay.

URSEnay.
Istress!may At,whay istress!may Uliet!jay Ast,fay Iay arrantway er,hay eshay.
Y,whay amb,lay y,whay ady,lay ie,fay youay ug-abed!slay
Y,whay ove,lay Iay ay!say Adam!may Eetheart!sway Y,whay ide!bray
At,whay otnay aay ord?way Youay aketay youray ennyworthspay ownay.
Eepslay orfay aay eek;way orfay ethay extnay ight,nay Iay arrant,way
Ethay Ountycay Arispay athhay etsay upay ishay estray

Elp,hay elp!hay Allcay elphay.

APULETcay.

Alackay ethay ay,day e’sshay ead,day e’sshay ead,day e’sshay ead!day

A!hay Etlay emay eesay erhay. Outay alas!ay E’sshay old,cay

URSEnay.
Oay amentablelay ay!day

ADYlay APULETcay.
Oay ofulway ime!tay

APULETcay.
Eath,day atthay athhay a’entay erhay encehay otay akemay emay ail,way

Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay anday Arispay ithway Usiciansmay.

IARfRay AWRENCElay.
Ome,cay isay ethay idebray eadyray otay ogay otay urch?chay

APULETcay.
Eadyray otay o,gay utbay evernay otay eturnray.
Oay on,say ethay ightnay eforebay ythay eddingway ayday
Athhay eathday ainlay ithway ythay idebray. Erethay eshay ies,lay
Owerflay asay eshay as,way efloweredday ybay imhay.
Eathday isay ymay on-in-law,say eathday isay ymay eir;hay
Ymay aughterday ehay athhay eddedway. Iay illway ieday
Anday eavelay imhay all;ay ife,lay iving,lay allay isay eath’sday.

ARISpay.
Avehay Iay oughtthay onglay otay eesay isthay orning’smay ace,fay
Anday othday itay ivegay emay uchsay aay ightsay asay is?thay

ADYlay APULETcay.
Accurs’d,ay unhappy,ay etched,wray atefulhay ayday.
Ostmay iserablemay ourhay atthay e’eray imetay awsay
Inay astinglay abourlay ofay ishay ilgrimagepay.
Utbay one,ay oorpay one,ay oneay oorpay anday ovinglay ild,chay
Utbay oneay ingthay otay ejoiceray anday olacesay in,ay
Anday uelcray eathday athhay atch’dcay itay omfray ymay ightsay.

URSEnay.
Oay oe!way Oay oeful,way oeful,way oefulway ayday.
Ostmay amentablelay ay,day ostmay oefulway ayday
Atthay ever,ay ever,ay Iay idday yetay ehold!bay
Oay ay,day Oay ay,day Oay ay,day Oay atefulhay ayday.
Evernay asway eensay osay ackblay aay ayday asay isthay.
Oay oefulway ay,day Oay oefulway ayday.

ARISpay.
Eguil’d,bay ivorced,day onged,wray ited,spay ainslay.
Ostmay etestableday eath,day ybay eethay eguil’d,bay
Ybay uel,cray uelcray eethay uiteqay overthrown.ay
Oay ove!lay Oay ife!lay Otnay ife,lay utbay ovelay inay eath!day

APULETcay.

Inay esethay onfusionscay. Eavenhay anday yourselfay
Adhay artpay inay isthay airfay aid,may ownay eavenhay athhay all,ay
Anday allay ethay etterbay isay itay orfay ethay aidmay.
Youray artpay inay erhay youay ouldcay otnay eepkay omfray eath,day

Aboveay ethay ouds,clay asay ighhay asay eavenhay itself?ay

ENEsCay I.ay Antuamay. Aay Eetstray.


Enteray Omeoray.

OMEOray.
Ifay Iay aymay usttray ethay atteringflay eyeay ofay eep,slay
Ymay eamsdray esagepray omesay oyfuljay ewsnay atay andhay.
Ymay osom’sbay ordlay itssay ightlylay inay ishay one;thray
Anday allay isthay ayday anay unaccustom’day iritspay
Iftslay emay aboveay ethay oundgray ithway eerfulchay oughtsthay.
Iay eamtdray ymay adylay amecay anday oundfay emay ead,—day
Angestray eam,dray atthay ivesgay aay eadday anmay eavelay otay ink!—thay
Anday eath’dbray uchsay ifelay ithway isseskay inay ymay ips,lay
Atthay Iay eviv’d,ray anday asway anay emperor.ay
Ahay e,may owhay eetsway isay ovelay itselfay ossess’d,pay
Enwhay utbay ove’slay adowsshay areay osay ichray inay oyjay.

Ell,way Uliet,jay Iay illway ielay ithway eethay onighttay.

Aay ightninglay eforebay eathday. O,ay owhay aymay Iay
Allcay isthay aay ightning?lay Oay ymay ove,lay ymay ife,way
Eathday atthay athhay uck’dsay ethay oneyhay ofay ythay eath,bray
Athhay adhay onay owerpay yetay uponay ythay eautybay.
Outhay artay otnay onquer’dcay. Eauty’sbay ensignay yetay
Isay imsoncray inay ythay ipslay anday inay ythay eeks,chay
Anday eath’sday alepay agflay isay otnay advanceday erethay.
Ybalt,tay iestlay outhay erethay inay ythay oodyblay eet?shay
O,ay atwhay oremay avourfay ancay Iay oday otay eethay
Anthay ithway atthay andhay atthay utcay ythay youthay inay aintway
Otay undersay ishay atthay asway inethay enemy?ay
Orgivefay e,may ousincay. Ah,ay earday Uliet,jay
Ywhay artay outhay yetay osay air?fay Allshay Iay elievebay
Atthay unsubstantialay eathday isay amorous;ay
Anday atthay ethay eanlay abhorreday onstermay eepskay
Eethay erehay inay arkday otay ebay ishay aramour?pay
Orfay earfay ofay atthay Iay illstay illway aystay ithway ee,thay
Anday evernay omfray isthay alacepay ofay imday ightnay
Epartday again.ay Ere,hay erehay illway Iay emainray
Ithway ormsway atthay areay ythay ambermaidschay. O,ay erehay
Illway Iay etsay upay ymay everlastingay est;ray
Anday akeshay ethay yokeay ofay inauspiciousay arsstay
Omfray isthay orld-weariedway eshflay. Eyes,ay ooklay youray astlay.
Arms,ay aketay youray astlay embrace!ay And,ay ips,lay Oay youay
Ethay oorsday ofay eath,bray ealsay ithway aay ighteousray isskay
Aay atelessday argainbay otay engrossingay eathday.
Ome,cay itterbay onduct,cay ome,cay unsavouryay uidegay.
Outhay esperateday ilot,pay ownay atay onceay unray onay
Ethay ashingday ocksray ythay ea-sicksay earyway arkbay.
Ere’shay otay ymay ove!lay Inks._][_Dray Oay uetray apothecary!ay
Ythay ugsdray areay uickqay. Usthay ithway aay isskay Iay ieday.
